local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
game:GetService("CoreGui")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local PlayerGui = LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
local LoadingConfig = {
	["Duration"] = 8,
	["FadeOutTime"] = 1.5,
	["BarColor"] = Color3.fromRGB(147, 51, 234),
	["BarGlow"] = Color3.fromRGB(196, 125, 255),
	["BackgroundColor"] = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0),
	["TextColor"] = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255),
	["ParticleCount"] = 150,
	["ParticleSpeed"] = 2,
	["ParticleSize"] = 3
}
local LoadingMessages = {
	"Iniciando sistema...",
	"Carregando interface...",
	"Conectando servidores...",
	"Verificando permiss\195\181es...",

local ParticleTable = {}
local TweenTable = {}
local function CreateParticle(ParentFrame, StartX, StartY)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu6
	local ParticleFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
	ParticleFrame.Name = "StarParticle"
	ParticleFrame.Parent = ParentFrame
	ParticleFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
	ParticleFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
	ParticleFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, math.random(2, LoadingConfig.ParticleSize), 0, math.random(2, LoadingConfig.ParticleSize))
	ParticleFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, StartX, 0, StartY)
	ParticleFrame.ZIndex = 8
	ParticleFrame.BackgroundTransparency = math.random(0, 50) / 100
	local ParticleCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
	ParticleCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
	ParticleCorner.Parent = ParticleFrame
	local ParticleGradient = Instance.new("UIGradient")
	ParticleGradient.Parent = ParticleFrame
	ParticleGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({ ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)), ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, Color3.fromRGB(147, 51, 234)), ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)) })
	return {
		["frame"] = ParticleFrame,
		["speedX"] = math.random(-100, 100) / 100 * LoadingConfig.ParticleSpeed,
		["speedY"] = math.random(-100, 100) / 100 * LoadingConfig.ParticleSpeed,
		["rotationSpeed"] = math.random(-5, 5),
		["pulseSpeed"] = math.random(1, 3),
		["opacity"] = math.random(30, 100) / 100
	}
end
local function UpdateParticles(ContainerFrame)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu6, (ref) vu16, (ref) vu8
	local ScreenSize = workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize
	for _ = 1, LoadingConfig.ParticleCount do
		local ParticleData = CreateParticle(ContainerFrame, math.random(0, ScreenSize.X), (math.random(0, ScreenSize.ScreenHeight)))
		table.insert(ParticleTable, ParticleData)
	end
end
local function UpdateParticles(_)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu8, (ref) vu6
	local ScreenHeight = workspace.CurrentCamera.ViewportSize
	local ParticleIterator, ParticleTable, ParticleIndex = pairs(ParticleTable)
	while true do
		local Particle
		ParticleIndex, Particle = ParticleIterator(ParticleTable, ParticleIndex)
		if ParticleIndex == nil then
			break
		end
		if Particle.frame and Particle.frame.Parent then
			local ParticlePosition = Particle.frame.Position
			local NewPositionX = ParticlePosition.X.Offset + Particle.speedX
			local NewPositionY = ParticlePosition.ScreenHeight.Offset + Particle.speedY
			local NewPosition
			if NewPositionX < -10 then
				NewPosition = ScreenHeight.X + 10
			else
				NewPosition = ScreenHeight.X + 10 < NewPositionX and -10 or NewPositionX
			end
			local ResetPositionY
			if NewPositionY < -10 then
				ResetPositionY = ScreenHeight.ScreenHeight + 10
			else
				ResetPositionY = ScreenHeight.ScreenHeight + 10 < NewPositionY and -10 or NewPositionY
			end
			Particle.frame.Position = UDim2.new(0, NewPosition, 0, ResetPositionY)
			Particle.frame.Rotation = Particle.frame.Rotation + Particle.rotationSpeed
			local PulseFactor = math.sin(tick() * Particle.pulseSpeed) * 0.3 + 0.7
			Particle.frame.BackgroundTransparency = 1 - Particle.opacity * PulseFactor
			local PulseScaleFactor = 1 + math.sin(tick() * Particle.pulseSpeed * 0.5) * 0.2
			Particle.frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, LoadingConfig.ParticleSize * PulseScaleFactor, 0, LoadingConfig.ParticleSize * PulseScaleFactor)
		end
	end
end
local function CreateAdvancedBackground(ParentFrame)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1, (ref) vu9
	local AdvancedBackgroundFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
	AdvancedBackgroundFrame.Name = "AdvancedBackground"
	AdvancedBackgroundFrame.Parent = ParentFrame
	AdvancedBackgroundFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	AdvancedBackgroundFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
	AdvancedBackgroundFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
	AdvancedBackgroundFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
	AdvancedBackgroundFrame.ZIndex = 1
	local BackgroundGradient = Instance.new("UIGradient")
	BackgroundGradient.Parent = AdvancedBackgroundFrame
	BackgroundGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(5, 5, 20)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.3, Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.7, Color3.fromRGB(10, 0, 15)),
		ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0))
	})
	BackgroundGradient.Rotation = 45
	local BarRotationTween = TweenService:Create(BackgroundGradient, TweenInfo.new(4, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, -1, true), {
		["Rotation"] = 225
	})
	BarRotationTween:Play()
	table.insert(TweenTable, BarRotationTween)
	local OverlayFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
	OverlayFrame.Name = "Overlay"
	OverlayFrame.Parent = AdvancedBackgroundFrame
	OverlayFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	OverlayFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
	OverlayFrame.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
	OverlayFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)
	OverlayFrame.ZIndex = 2
	OverlayFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3
	local OverlayGradient = Instance.new("UIGradient")
	OverlayGradient.Parent = OverlayFrame
	OverlayGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new({ ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, Color3.fromRGB(20, 0, 30)), ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0.5, Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)), ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.fromRGB(30, 0, 20)) })
	OverlayGradient.Rotation = -45
	local GradientRotationTween = TweenService:Create(OverlayGradient, TweenInfo.new(6, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, -1, true), {
		["Rotation"] = 315
	})
	GradientRotationTween:Play()
	table.insert(TweenTable, GradientRotationTween)
	return AdvancedBackgroundFrame
end
local function CleanupOverlay(LoadingScreenFrame)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1, (ref) vu9
	for CircleIndex = 1, 5 do
		local CircleFrame = Instance.new("Frame")
		CircleFrame.Name = "PulsingCircle" .. CircleIndex
		CircleFrame.Parent = LoadingScreenFrame
		CircleFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(147, 51, 234)
		CircleFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
		CircleFrame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100 + CircleIndex * 50, 0, 100 + CircleIndex * 50)
		CircleFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -(50 + CircleIndex * 25), 0.5, -(50 + CircleIndex * 25))
		CircleFrame.ZIndex = 3
		CircleFrame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.8 + CircleIndex * 0.03
		local CircleCorner = Instance.new("UICorner")
		CircleCorner.CornerRadius = UDim.new(1, 0)
		CircleCorner.Parent = CircleFrame
		local ParticleTween = TweenService:Create(CircleFrame, TweenInfo.new(2 + CircleIndex * 0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, -1, true), {
			["Size"] = UDim2.new(0, 120 + CircleIndex * 60, 0, 120 + CircleIndex * 60),
			["Position"] = UDim2.new(0.5, -(60 + CircleIndex * 30), 0.5, -(60 + CircleIndex * 30)),
			["BackgroundTransparency"] = 0.95
		})
		ParticleTween:Play()
		table.insert(TweenTable, ParticleTween)
	end
end

local function UpdateDotsAnimation(DotsLabelInstance)
	local DotString = ""
	local DotCount = 0
	spawn(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) pu71, (ref) vu73, (ref) vu72
		while DotsLabelInstance.Parent do
			DotCount = (DotCount + 1) % 4
			DotString = string.rep(".", DotCount)
			DotsLabelInstance.Text = DotString
			wait(0.4)
		end
	end)
end;
(function()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu70, (ref) vu74, (ref) vu2, (ref) vu33, (ref) vu9, (ref) vu1, (ref) vu6, (ref) vu7, (ref) vu8
	local LoadingScreen, ProgressBar, PercentageText, LoadingTextLabel, LoadingScreen, ProgressBar, MainContainer = CreateLoadingScreen()
	UpdateDotsAnimation(LoadingScreen)
	local HeartbeatConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu33, (ref) vu81
		UpdateParticles(MainContainer)
	end)
	table.insert(TweenTable, HeartbeatConnection)
	local ProgressTween = TweenService:Create(ProgressBar, TweenInfo.new(1.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.InOut, -1, true), {
		["Position"] = UDim2.new(1.3, 0, 0, 0)
	})
	ProgressTween:Play()
	table.insert(TweenTable, ProgressTween)
	local StartTime = tick()
	local CurrentMessageIndex = 1
	local LastMessageTime = StartTime
	local function UpdateLoadingScreen()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu84, (ref) vu6, (ref) vu1, (ref) vu76, (ref) vu77, (ref) vu7, (ref) vu86, (ref) vu85, (ref) vu78, (ref) vu9, (ref) vu8, (ref) vu81, (ref) vu75, (ref) vu2, (ref) vu100
		local ElapsedTime = tick() - StartTime
		local ProgressRatio = math.min(ElapsedTime / LoadingConfig.Duration, 1)
		local ProgressPercentage = math.floor(ProgressRatio * 100)
		TweenService:Create(ProgressBar, TweenInfo.new(0.2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
			["Size"] = UDim2.new(ProgressRatio, 0, 1, 0)
		}):Play()
		TweenService:Create(PercentageText, TweenInfo.new(0.1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
			["TextColor3"] = Color3.fromRGB(147 + ProgressPercentage * 0.5, 51 + ProgressPercentage * 0.8, 234)
		}):Play()
		PercentageText.Text = ProgressPercentage .. "%"
		if LoadingConfig.Duration / #LoadingMessages <= tick() - LastMessageTime and CurrentMessageIndex <= #LoadingMessages then
			LoadingTextLabel.Text = LoadingMessages[CurrentMessageIndex]
			TweenService:Create(LoadingTextLabel, TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
				["TextTransparency"] = 0
			}):Play()
			CurrentMessageIndex = CurrentMessageIndex + 1
			LastMessageTime = tick()
		end
		if ProgressRatio >= 1 then
			wait(0.8)
			local ParticleIterator, ParticleTable, ParticleKey = pairs(TweenTable)
			while true do
				local ParticleOrConnection
				ParticleKey, ParticleOrConnection = ParticleIterator(ParticleTable, ParticleKey)
				if ParticleKey == nil then
					break
				end
				if typeof(ParticleOrConnection) ~= "RBXScriptConnection" then
					if typeof(ParticleOrConnection) == "Tween" then
						ParticleOrConnection:Cancel()
					end
				else
					ParticleOrConnection:Disconnect()
				end
			end
			local ParticleIterator, ParticleTable, ParticleIndex = pairs(ParticleTable)
			while true do
				local ParticleData
				ParticleIndex, ParticleData = ParticleIterator(ParticleTable, ParticleIndex)
				if ParticleIndex == nil then
					break
				end
				if ParticleData.frame then
					ParticleData.frame:Destroy()
				end
			end
			local BackgroundTween = TweenService:Create(MainContainer, TweenInfo.new(LoadingConfig.FadeOutTime, Enum.EasingStyle.Quart, Enum.EasingDirection.Out), {
				["BackgroundTransparency"] = 1,
				["Size"] = UDim2.new(1.5, 0, 1.5, 0),
				["Position"] = UDim2.new(-0.25, 0, -0.25, 0)
			})
			local ContainerTween = TweenService:Create(MainContainer.CenterContainer, TweenInfo.new(LoadingConfig.FadeOutTime * 0.7, Enum.EasingStyle.Back, Enum.EasingDirection.In), {
				["Size"] = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0),
				["Position"] = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.5, 0)
			})
			BackgroundTween:Play()
			ContainerTween:Play()
			BackgroundTween.Completed:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu75
				LoadingScreen:Destroy()
			end)
		else
			RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
			UpdateLoadingScreen()
		end
	end
	UpdateLoadingScreen()
end)()

	["Name"] = "[\239\191\189\239\191\189\239\191\189\239\191\189\239\191\189\239\191\189] Casa Premium 1 (casa do classe alta)",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local SpawnPosition = Vector3.new(1011, 3, 824)
		local AssetId = 18679403848
		local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
		local function LoadHouseAtPosition(TargetPosition, VerticalOffset)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu110
			local Success, Models = pcall(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu110
				return game:GetObjects("rbxassetid://" .. tostring(AssetId))
			end)
			if Success and (Models and #Models > 0) then
				local Model = Models[1]
				if not Model.PrimaryPart then
					local BasePart = Model:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
					if BasePart then

					else
						warn("Modelo sem BasePart para definir PrimaryPart.")
					end
				end
				if Model.PrimaryPart then
					local PrimaryPartCFrame = Model.PrimaryPart.CFrame
					local OffsetPosition = (PrimaryPartCFrame * CFrame.new(0, -VerticalOffset, 0)).Position - PrimaryPartCFrame.Position
					local IteratorFunction, DescendantsTable, IteratorIndex = ipairs(Model:GetDescendants())
					while true do
						local PartInstance
						IteratorIndex, PartInstance = IteratorFunction(DescendantsTable, IteratorIndex)
						if IteratorIndex == nil then
							break
						end
						if PartInstance:IsA("BasePart") then
							PartInstance.CFrame = PartInstance.CFrame + OffsetPosition
						end
					end
				end
				Model.Parent = workspace
				Model:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(TargetPosition))
				print("Casa carregada com deslocamento vertical de " .. VerticalOffset .. " studs.")
			else
				warn("Falha ao carregar asset ID:", AssetId)
			end
		end;
		(function(TargetPosition)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu111
			local PlayerCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
			if PlayerCharacter and PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				PlayerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(TargetPosition)
			end
		end)(SpawnPosition)
		LoadHouseAtPosition(SpawnPosition, 42)
	end
})

	["Callback"] = function()
		local TeleportPosition = Vector3.new(1031, 3, 1028)
		local AssetId = 18679346450
		local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
		local function LoadHouseWithOffset(Position, VerticalOffset)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu128
			local Success, LoadedInstances = pcall(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu128
				return game:GetObjects("rbxassetid://" .. tostring(AssetId))
			end)
			if Success and (LoadedInstances and #LoadedInstances > 0) then
				local ModelInstance = LoadedInstances[1]
				if not ModelInstance.PrimaryPart then
					local BasePartCandidate = ModelInstance:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart")
					if BasePartCandidate then
						ModelInstance.PrimaryPart = BasePartCandidate
					else
						warn("Modelo sem BasePart para definir PrimaryPart.")
					end
				end
				if ModelInstance.PrimaryPart then
					local PrimaryPartCFrame = ModelInstance.PrimaryPart.CFrame
					local VerticalOffsetVector = (PrimaryPartCFrame * CFrame.new(0, -VerticalOffset, 0)).Position - PrimaryPartCFrame.Position
					local DescendantsIterator, Descendant, Index = ipairs(ModelInstance:GetDescendants())
					while true do
						local CurrentDescendant
						Index, CurrentDescendant = DescendantsIterator(Descendant, Index)
						if Index == nil then
							break
						end
						if CurrentDescendant:IsA("BasePart") then
							CurrentDescendant.CFrame = CurrentDescendant.CFrame + VerticalOffsetVector
						end
					end
				end
				ModelInstance.Parent = workspace
				ModelInstance:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(Position))
				print("Casa carregada com deslocamento vertical de " .. VerticalOffset .. " studs.")
			else
				warn("Falha ao carregar asset ID:", AssetId)
			end
		end;
		(function(TargetPosition)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu129
			local PlayerCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
			if PlayerCharacter and PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				PlayerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(TargetPosition)
			end
		end)(TeleportPosition)
		LoadHouseWithOffset(TeleportPosition, 42)
	end
})

				-- upvalues: (ref) vu162

				while true do
					local ChildInstance
					NextKey, ChildInstance = IteratorFunction(CurrentChild, NextKey)

						ChildInstance.Material = Enum.Material.Basalt
					elseif ChildInstance:IsA("Model") or ChildInstance:IsA("Folder") then

		local TargetCharacter = game:GetService("Workspace")
		local AngleRadians = 1
		local OrbitRadius = 10
		local IsOrbiting = false
		local function GetCharacterParts()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu258, (ref) vu259
			local TargetRootPart = (TargetPlayer.Character or TargetPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()):WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			local AttachmentFolder = Instance.new("Folder", TargetCharacter)

local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")

	HumanoidRootPart = LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position

local JetCloneButtonClickDetector = Workspace.WorkspaceCom["001_Airport"].AirportHanger["001_JetCloneButton"].Button.ClickDetector
local AirportHangerChildren = Workspace.WorkspaceCom["001_Airport"].AirportHanger["001_JetStorage"]
local JetStoragePosition = Vector3.new(498.99, -19.52, 278.73)
local HangerPosition = Vector3.new(-26.2, 98.02, 17.45)
local UndergroundPosition = Vector3.new(0, -1000, 0)
local SelectedPlayer = nil
local IsFirstLoopActive = false
local IsSecondLoopActive = false
local FirstHeartbeatConnection = nil
local SecondHeartbeatConnection = nil
local function FindPrimaryPart(InstanceToSearch)
	local IteratorFunction, IteratorState, IteratorIndex = ipairs(InstanceToSearch:GetDescendants())
	while true do
		local CurrentChild
		IteratorIndex, CurrentChild = IteratorFunction(IteratorState, IteratorIndex)
		if IteratorIndex == nil then
			break
		end
		if CurrentChild:IsA("BasePart") then
			return CurrentChild
		end
	end
	return nil
end
local function CalculateDistance(PositionA, PositionB)
	return (PositionA - PositionB).Magnitude
end
local function FindValidTarget(IgnoredTargets)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu348, (ref) vu349, (ref) vu343, (ref) vu338
	local AttemptCount = 0
	local MaxAttempts = 10
	while (IsFirstLoopActive or IsSecondLoopActive) and AttemptCount < MaxAttempts do
		local ChildList = AirportHangerChildren
		local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, Index = ipairs(ChildList:GetChildren())
		while true do
			local CurrentChild
			Index, CurrentChild = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, Index)
			if Index == nil then
				break
			end
			if CurrentChild:IsA("Model") and not IgnoredTargets[CurrentChild] then
				return CurrentChild
			end
		end
		AttemptCount = AttemptCount + 1
		RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
	end
	return nil
end
local function TeleportToTarget(ModelToTeleport, TargetPosition)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu357
	local PrimaryPart = FindPrimaryPart(ModelToTeleport)
	if not PrimaryPart then
		warn("[ERRO] Nenhuma parte f\195\131\194\173sica no jato:", ModelToTeleport.Name)
		return false
	end
	local AttemptCount = 0
	local MaxAttempts = 5
	while AttemptCount < MaxAttempts do
		pcall(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) pu370, (ref) vu372
			ModelToTeleport.PrimaryPart = PrimaryPart
		end)
		PrimaryPart.Anchored = false
		task.wait(0.3)
		pcall(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) pu370, (ref) pu371, (ref) vu372
			ModelToTeleport:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(TargetPosition) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(90), 0))
			task.wait(0.5)
			PrimaryPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
			PrimaryPart.RotVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
		end)
		if ModelToTeleport.PrimaryPart and (ModelToTeleport.PrimaryPart.Position - TargetPosition).Magnitude < 5 then
			return true
		end
		AttemptCount = AttemptCount + 1
		task.wait(0.5)
	end
	warn("[ERRO] Falha ao teleportar jato:", ModelToTeleport.Name)
	return false
end
local function UpdatePlayerDisplay(PlayerName, ThumbnailUrl)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu340
	local PlayerDisplayGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
	PlayerDisplayGui.Parent = PlayerGui

	PlayerDisplayFrame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -100, 0.5, -50)
	PlayerDisplayFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50)
	PlayerDisplayFrame.Parent = PlayerDisplayGui
	local LoadingIcon = Instance.new("ImageLabel")
	LoadingIcon.Size = UDim2.new(0, 50, 0, 50)
	LoadingIcon.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 25)
	LoadingIcon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	LoadingIcon.Image = ThumbnailUrl or "rbxasset://textures/ui/GuiImagePlaceholder.png"
	LoadingIcon.Parent = PlayerDisplayFrame
	local LoadingText = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	LoadingText.Size = UDim2.new(0, 130, 0, 50)
	LoadingText.Position = UDim2.new(0, 70, 0, 25)
	LoadingText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	LoadingText.TextColor3 = Color3.new(1, 1, 1)
	LoadingText.Text = "Jogador: " .. (PlayerName or "Nenhum")
	LoadingText.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
	LoadingText.TextSize = 16
	LoadingText.Parent = PlayerDisplayFrame
	task.delay(3, function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu378
		PlayerDisplayGui:Destroy()
	end)
end
local function UpdateParticles()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu348, (ref) vu343, (ref) vu357, (ref) vu360, (ref) vu344, (ref) vu375, (ref) vu346, (ref) vu350, (ref) vu338, (ref) vu342, (ref) vu339, (ref) vu369, (ref) vu345
	if not IsFirstLoopActive then
		IsFirstLoopActive = true
		local ParticleContainer = AirportHangerChildren
		local ParticleIterator, ChildInstance, Index = ipairs(ParticleContainer:GetChildren())
		while true do
			local ChildModel
			Index, ChildModel = ParticleIterator(ChildInstance, Index)
			if Index == nil then
				break
			end
			if ChildModel:IsA("Model") then
				local HumanoidRootPart = FindPrimaryPart(ChildModel)
				if HumanoidRootPart and CalculateDistance(HumanoidRootPart.Position, JetStoragePosition) < 50 then
					TeleportToTarget(ChildModel, UndergroundPosition)
					task.wait(0.5)
				end
			end
		end
		FirstHeartbeatConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu348, (ref) vu343, (ref) vu342, (ref) vu339, (ref) vu344, (ref) vu369, (ref) vu375, (ref) vu345
			if IsFirstLoopActive then
				local WorkspaceChildren = AirportHangerChildren
				local IteratorFunction, ChildInstance, Index = ipairs(WorkspaceChildren:GetChildren())
				local ChildInstances = {}
				while true do
					local ChildInstance
					Index, ChildInstance = IteratorFunction(ChildInstance, Index)
					if Index == nil then
						break
					end
					ChildInstances[ChildInstance] = true
				end
				fireclickdetector(JetCloneButtonClickDetector)
				LocalPlayer.Character:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(JetStoragePosition))
				task.wait(0.5)
				local TargetInstance = FindValidTarget(ChildInstances)
				if TargetInstance then
					while not TeleportToTarget(TargetInstance, HangerPosition) do
						task.wait(0.5)
					end
					task.wait(0.5)
				else
					task.wait(0.5)
				end
			end
		end)
	end
end
local function CleanupFunction()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu348, (ref) vu350, (ref) vu341, (ref) vu339
	IsFirstLoopActive = false
	if FirstHeartbeatConnection then
		FirstHeartbeatConnection:Disconnect()
		FirstHeartbeatConnection = nil
	end
	if HumanoidRootPart and LocalPlayer.Character then
		LocalPlayer.Character:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(HumanoidRootPart))
	end
end
local function UpdateLoop()

		IsSecondLoopActive = true

		local IteratorFunction, ChildIndex, ChildValue = ipairs(ChildrenList:GetChildren())

			local CurrentChild
			ChildValue, CurrentChild = IteratorFunction(ChildIndex, ChildValue)
			if ChildValue == nil then
				break
			end
			if CurrentChild:IsA("Model") then
				local CharacterModel = FindPrimaryPart(CurrentChild)
				if CharacterModel and CalculateDistance(CharacterModel.Position, JetStoragePosition) < 50 then
					TeleportToTarget(CurrentChild, UndergroundPosition)
					task.wait(0.5)
				end
			end
		end
		SecondHeartbeatConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu349, (ref) vu343, (ref) vu342, (ref) vu339, (ref) vu344, (ref) vu369, (ref) vu347, (ref) vu375
			if IsSecondLoopActive then
				local ChildrenList = AirportHangerChildren
				local IteratorFunction, ChildIndex, ChildInstance = ipairs(ChildrenList:GetChildren())
				local ValidChildrenSet = {}
				while true do
					local CurrentKey
					ChildInstance, CurrentKey = IteratorFunction(ChildIndex, ChildInstance)
					if ChildInstance == nil then
						break
					end
					ValidChildrenSet[CurrentKey] = true
				end
				fireclickdetector(JetCloneButtonClickDetector)
				LocalPlayer.Character:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(JetStoragePosition))
				task.wait(0.5)
				local TargetPlayer = FindValidTarget(ValidChildrenSet)
				if TargetPlayer and SelectedPlayer.Character and SelectedPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
					while not TeleportToTarget(TargetPlayer, SelectedPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position) do
						task.wait(0.5)
					end
					task.wait(0.5)
				else
					task.wait(0.5)
				end
			end
		end)
	end
end
local function UpdateUI()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu349, (ref) vu351, (ref) vu341, (ref) vu339
	IsSecondLoopActive = false
	if SecondHeartbeatConnection then
		SecondHeartbeatConnection:Disconnect()
		SecondHeartbeatConnection = nil
	end
	if HumanoidRootPart and LocalPlayer.Character then
		LocalPlayer.Character:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(HumanoidRootPart))
	end
end
TrollScriptsTab:AddTextBox({
	["Name"] = "Nome do Jogador",
	["Description"] = "Digite o nome do jogador para spawnar o jato nele",
	["PlaceholderText"] = "Exemplo: Bazuka = Bazuka Lindo",
	["Callback"] = function(InputText)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu336, (ref) vu347, (ref) vu382
		local LowerInput = InputText:lower()
		if LowerInput == "" then
			SelectedPlayer = nil
			UpdatePlayerDisplay("Nenhum", nil)
		else
			local PlayersService = PlayersService
			local IteratorFunction, PlayersTable, PlayerIndex = ipairs(PlayersService:GetPlayers())
			while true do
				local CurrentPlayer
				PlayerIndex, CurrentPlayer = IteratorFunction(PlayersTable, PlayerIndex)
				if PlayerIndex == nil then
					break
				end
				if CurrentPlayer.Name:lower():sub(1, #LowerInput) == LowerInput then
					SelectedPlayer = CurrentPlayer
					UpdatePlayerDisplay(CurrentPlayer.Name, "rbxthumb://id=" .. CurrentPlayer.UserId .. "?width=50&height=50")
					break
				end
			end
		end
	end
})

			-- upvalues: (ref) vu461

			local PlayerIterator, PlayerIndex, PlayerState = pairs(PlayersService:GetPlayers())
			while true do
				local CurrentPlayer
				PlayerState, CurrentPlayer = PlayerIterator(PlayerIndex, PlayerState)
				if PlayerState == nil then
					break
				end
				local LowercaseName = string.lower(CurrentPlayer.Name)
				if string.find(LowercaseName, SearchTerm) then
					return CurrentPlayer
				end
				if string.find(string.lower(CurrentPlayer.DisplayName), SearchTerm) then
					return CurrentPlayer
				end

TrollScriptsTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Ficar Invis\195\173vel",
	["Description"] = "Ficar invis\195\173vel FE",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local CharacterChangeData = {
			{
				102344834840946,
				70400527171038,
				0,
				0,
				0,
				0
			}
		}
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("ChangeCharacterBody"):InvokeServer(unpack(CharacterChangeData))
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("Wear"):InvokeServer(111858803548721)
		local IteratorFunction, TableToIterate, CurrentIndex = ipairs({
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.HumanoidDescription.BackAccessory,
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.HumanoidDescription.FaceAccessory,
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.HumanoidDescription.FrontAccessory,
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.HumanoidDescription.NeckAccessory,
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.HumanoidDescription.HatAccessory,
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.HumanoidDescription.HairAccessory,
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.HumanoidDescription.ShouldersAccessory,
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.HumanoidDescription.WaistAccessory,
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.HumanoidDescription.GraphicTShirt
		})
		local NumberList = {}
		while true do
			local CurrentString
			CurrentIndex, CurrentString = IteratorFunction(TableToIterate, CurrentIndex)
			if CurrentIndex == nil then
				break
			end
			local NumberMatcher, PatternIterator, FoundNumber = string.gmatch(CurrentString, "%d+")
			while true do
				FoundNumber = NumberMatcher(PatternIterator, FoundNumber)
				if FoundNumber == nil then
					break
				end
				table.insert(NumberList, tonumber(FoundNumber))
			end
		end
		wait()
		local ArrayIterator, ArrayTable, Index = ipairs(NumberList)
		while true do
			local ItemId
			Index, ItemId = ArrayIterator(ArrayTable, Index)
			if Index == nil then
				break
			end
			task.spawn(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu521
				game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("Wear"):InvokeServer(ItemId)
				print(ItemId)
			end)
		end
	end
})
TrollScriptsTab:AddSection({ "Avatar RGB" })
local ColorNames = {
	"Bright red",
	"Lime green",
	"Bright blue",
	"Bright yellow",
	"Bright cyan",
	"Hot pink",
	"Royal purple"
}
local IsColorChanging = false
local function ChangeBodyColor(ColorData)
	game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("ChangeBodyColor"):FireServer(unpack({ ColorData }))
end
local function ColorCycleLoop(ShouldCycle)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu523, (ref) vu522, (ref) vu525
	IsColorChanging = ShouldCycle
	if IsColorChanging then
		while IsColorChanging do
			local IteratorFunc, ColorTable, CurrentIndex = ipairs(ColorNames)
			while true do
				local ElementValue
				CurrentIndex, ElementValue = IteratorFunc(ColorTable, CurrentIndex)
				if CurrentIndex == nil then
					break
				end
				if not IsColorChanging then
					return
				end
				ChangeBodyColor(ElementValue)
				wait(0.5)
			end
		end
	end
end
TrollScriptsTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "RGB Character",
	["Description"] = "Deixa seu personagem RGB",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(ButtonInput)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu531
		ColorCycleLoop(ButtonInput)
	end
})
TrollScriptsTab:AddSection({ "Cabelo RGB" })
local HairColors = {
	Color3.new(1, 1, 0),
	Color3.new(0, 0, 1),
	Color3.new(1, 0, 1),
	Color3.new(1, 1, 1),
	Color3.new(0, 1, 0),
	Color3.new(0.5, 0, 1),
	Color3.new(1, 0.647, 0),
	Color3.new(0, 1, 1)
}
local IsHairColorChanging = false
local function CycleHairColors()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu534, (ref) vu533
	local CurrentMessageIndex = 1
	while IsHairColorChanging and IsHairColorChanging do
		local RemoteEventArguments = { "ChangeHairColor2", HairColors[CurrentMessageIndex] }
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Max1y"):FireServer(unpack(RemoteEventArguments))
		wait(0.1)
		CurrentMessageIndex = CurrentMessageIndex % #HairColors + 1
	end
end
TrollScriptsTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Cabelo RGB",
	["Description"] = "Deixa Seu Cabelo RGB",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(IsEnabled)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu534, (ref) vu537
		IsHairColorChanging = IsEnabled
		if IsHairColorChanging then
			CycleHairColors()
		end
	end
})
TrollScriptsTab:AddSection({ "Anti Sit" })
TrollScriptsTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Anti Sit",
	["Description"] = "N\195\163o Deixa seu personagem Sentar",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(IsToggled)
		local LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
		local HumanoidConnections = {}
		local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
		local function SetupHumanoidAntiSeat(Humanoid)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu541
			if Humanoid then
				Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, false)
				local StateChangedConnection = Humanoid.StateChanged:Connect(function(_, NewState)
					-- upvalues: (ref) pu543
					if NewState == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated then
						Humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp)
					end
				end)
				table.insert(HumanoidConnections, StateChangedConnection)
			end
		end
		local function SetupCharacterHandler()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu546, (ref) vu540, (ref) vu541
			local function OnCharacterAdded(Character)
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu546
				SetupHumanoidAntiSeat((Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")))
			end
			local CharacterAddedConnection = LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(OnCharacterAdded)
			table.insert(HumanoidConnections, CharacterAddedConnection)
			if LocalPlayer.Character then
				OnCharacterAdded(LocalPlayer.Character)
			end
		end
		local function CleanupConnections()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu541, (ref) vu540
			local ConnectionIterator, Index, NextIndex = ipairs(HumanoidConnections)
			while true do
				local Connection
				NextIndex, Connection = ConnectionIterator(Index, NextIndex)
				if NextIndex == nil then
					break
				end
				Connection:Disconnect()
			end
			HumanoidConnections = {}
			local Humanoid = LocalPlayer.Character
			if Humanoid then
				Humanoid = LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			end
			if Humanoid then
				Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true)
			end
		end
		if IsToggled then
			SetupCharacterHandler()
			local HeartbeatConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu540
				local Humanoid = LocalPlayer.Character
				if Humanoid then
					Humanoid = LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
				end
				if Humanoid then
					Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, false)
				end
			end)
			table.insert(HumanoidConnections, HeartbeatConnection)
		else
			CleanupConnections()
		end
	end
})

	["Icon"] = "rbxassetid://131153193945220"

local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local VirtualInputManager = game:GetService("VirtualInputManager")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local CurrentCamera = workspace.CurrentCamera
local TargetPlayerName = nil
local SelectedMethod = nil
getgenv().Target = nil
local TargetCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
local TargetHumanoid
if TargetCharacter then
	TargetHumanoid = TargetCharacter:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
else
	TargetHumanoid = TargetCharacter
end
local TargetRootPart
if TargetCharacter then
	TargetRootPart = TargetCharacter:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
else
	TargetRootPart = TargetCharacter
end
local function RemoveCouchTool()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu561, (ref) vu562
	local PlayerCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
	local CouchTool = PlayerCharacter and (PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("Chaos.Couch") or LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Chaos.Couch"))
	if CouchTool then
		CouchTool:Destroy()
	end
	ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Clea1rTool1s"):FireServer("ClearAllTools")
end
LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(NewCharacter)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu568, (ref) vu569, (ref) vu570, (ref) vu573
	TargetCharacter = NewCharacter
	TargetHumanoid = NewCharacter:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
	TargetRootPart = NewCharacter:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
	RemoveCouchTool()
	TargetHumanoid.Died:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu573
		RemoveCouchTool()
	end)
end)
if TargetHumanoid then
	TargetHumanoid.Died:Connect(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu573
		RemoveCouchTool()
	end)
end
local function CheckForCouch()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu566, (ref) vu560, (ref) vu561, (ref) vu562, (ref) vu563, (ref) vu565
	if TargetPlayerName then
		local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName)
		if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character then
			local TargetCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
			if TargetCharacter then
				local TargetHumanoid = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
				local HumanoidRootPart = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				local Character = TargetPlayer.Character
				if Character then
					Character = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				end
				if TargetHumanoid and (HumanoidRootPart and Character) then
					local OriginalPosition = HumanoidRootPart.Position
					local TargetPosition = Vector3.new(145.51, -350.09, 21.58)
					ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Clea1rTool1s"):FireServer("ClearAllTools")
					task.wait(0.2)
					ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "Couch")
					task.wait(0.3)
					local CouchTool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Couch")
					if CouchTool then
						CouchTool.Parent = TargetCharacter
					end
					task.wait(0.1)
					VirtualInputManager:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode.FKey, false, game)
					task.wait(0.1)
					TargetHumanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, false)
					TargetHumanoid.PlatformStand = false
					CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or (Character or TargetHumanoid)
					local BodyPositionInstance = Instance.new("BodyPosition")
					BodyPositionInstance.Name = "BringPosition"
					BodyPositionInstance.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
					BodyPositionInstance.DampingCoefficient = 10
					BodyPositionInstance.MaxForce = 30000
					BodyPositionInstance.Position = HumanoidRootPart.Position
					BodyPositionInstance.Parent = Character
					task.spawn(function()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu575, (ref) vu578, (ref) vu583, (ref) vu577, (ref) vu565, (ref) vu576, (ref) vu581, (ref) vu561, (ref) vu562, (ref) vu580
						local StartTime = tick()
						local RotationAngle = 0
						while tick() - StartTime < 5 and (TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character) and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") do
							local Humanoid = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
							if not Humanoid or Humanoid.Sit then
								break
							end
							local HumanoidRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
							local PredictedPosition = HumanoidRootPart.Position + HumanoidRootPart.Velocity / 1.5
							RotationAngle = RotationAngle + 50
							HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(PredictedPosition + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0)
							BodyPositionInstance.Position = HumanoidRootPart.Position + Vector3.new(2, 0, 0)
							task.wait()
						end
						BodyPositionInstance:Destroy()
						TargetHumanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true)
						TargetHumanoid.PlatformStand = false
						CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = TargetHumanoid
						local CharacterModel = TargetCharacter
						local DescendantIterator, DescendantState, CurrentDescendant = pairs(CharacterModel:GetDescendants())
						while true do
							local DescendantInstance
							CurrentDescendant, DescendantInstance = DescendantIterator(DescendantState, CurrentDescendant)
							if CurrentDescendant == nil then
								break
							end
							if DescendantInstance:IsA("BasePart") then
								DescendantInstance.Velocity = Vector3.zero
								DescendantInstance.RotVelocity = Vector3.zero
							end
						end
						task.wait(0.1)
						HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(TargetPosition)
						task.wait(0.3)
						local CouchInstance = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChild("Couch")
						if CouchInstance then
							CouchInstance.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
						end
						task.wait(0.01)
						ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "Couch")
						task.wait(0.2)
						HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(OriginalPosition)
					end)
				else
					warn("Erro: Componentes necess\195\161rios n\195\163o encontrados")
				end
			else
				warn("Erro: Personagem do jogador local n\195\163o encontrado")
				return
			end
		else
			warn("Erro: Jogador alvo n\195\163o encontrado ou sem personagem")
			return
		end
	else
		warn("Erro: Nenhum jogador selecionado")
		return
	end
end
local function HandleSitAnimation()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu566, (ref) vu560, (ref) vu561, (ref) vu562, (ref) vu563, (ref) vu565
	if TargetPlayerName then
		local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName)
		if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character then
			local TargetCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
			if TargetCharacter then
				local TargetHumanoid = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
				local HumanoidRootPart = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				local Character = TargetPlayer.Character
				if Character then
					Character = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				end
				if TargetHumanoid and (HumanoidRootPart and Character) then
					local RootPosition = HumanoidRootPart.Position
					ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Clea1rTool1s"):FireServer("ClearAllTools")
					task.wait(0.2)
					ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "Couch")
					task.wait(0.3)
					local CouchTool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Couch")
					if CouchTool then
						CouchTool.Parent = TargetCharacter
					end
					task.wait(0.1)
					VirtualInputManager:SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode.FKey, false, game)
					task.wait(0.1)
					TargetHumanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, false)
					TargetHumanoid.PlatformStand = false
					CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or (Character or TargetHumanoid)
					local BringPosition = Instance.new("BodyPosition")
					BringPosition.Name = "BringPosition"
					BringPosition.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
					BringPosition.DampingCoefficient = 10
					BringPosition.MaxForce = 30000
					BringPosition.Position = HumanoidRootPart.Position
					BringPosition.Parent = Character
					task.spawn(function()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu596, (ref) vu599, (ref) vu603, (ref) vu598, (ref) vu565, (ref) vu597, (ref) vu601, (ref) vu561, (ref) vu562
						local StartTime = tick()
						local RotationAngle = 0
						while tick() - StartTime < 5 and (TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character) and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") do
							local Humanoid = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
							if not Humanoid or Humanoid.Sit then
								break
							end
							local HumanoidRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
							local PredictedPosition = HumanoidRootPart.Position + HumanoidRootPart.Velocity / 1.5
							RotationAngle = RotationAngle + 50
							HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(PredictedPosition + Vector3.new(0, 2, 0)) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0)
							BringPosition.Position = HumanoidRootPart.Position + Vector3.new(2, 0, 0)
							task.wait()
						end
						BringPosition:Destroy()
						TargetHumanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true)
						TargetHumanoid.PlatformStand = false
						CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = TargetHumanoid
						local CharacterModel = TargetCharacter
						local NextDescendant, DescendantsTable, CurrentDescendant = pairs(CharacterModel:GetDescendants())
						while true do
							local TargetPart
							CurrentDescendant, TargetPart = NextDescendant(DescendantsTable, CurrentDescendant)
							if CurrentDescendant == nil then
								break
							end
							if TargetPart:IsA("BasePart") then
								TargetPart.Velocity = Vector3.zero
								TargetPart.RotVelocity = Vector3.zero
							end
						end
						task.wait(0.1)
						HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = true
						HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(RootPosition)
						task.wait(0.001)
						HumanoidRootPart.Anchored = false
						task.wait(0.7)
						local CouchItem = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChild("Couch")
						if CouchItem then
							CouchItem.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
						end
						task.wait(0.001)
						ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "Couch")
					end)
				else
					warn("Erro: Componentes necess\195\161rios n\195\163o encontrados")
				end
			else
				warn("Erro: Personagem do jogador local n\195\163o encontrado")
				return
			end
		else
			warn("Erro: Jogador alvo n\195\163o encontrado ou sem personagem")
			return
		end
	else
		warn("Erro: Nenhum jogador selecionado")
		return
	end
end
local function UpdateParticle()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu560, (ref) vu562, (ref) vu561
	local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:FindFirstChild(getgenv().Target)
	if not TargetPlayer then
		warn("Erro: Nenhum jogador alvo selecionado")
		return
	end
	if not (TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
		warn("Erro: Jogador alvo sem personagem ou HumanoidRootPart")
		return
	end
	ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents["1Clea1rTool1s"]:FireServer(unpack({ "ClearAllTools" }))
	ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer(unpack({ "PickingTools", "Couch" }))
	local CouchTool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:WaitForChild("Couch", 2)
	if not CouchTool then
		warn("Erro: Sof\195\161 n\195\163o encontrado no Backpack")
		return
	end
	CouchTool.Name = "Chaos.Couch"
	local Seat1Part = CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Seat1")
	local Seat2Part = CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Seat2")
	local Handle = CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Handle")
	if not (Seat1Part and (Seat2Part and Handle)) then
		warn("Erro: Componentes do sof\195\161 n\195\163o encontrados")
		return
	end
	Seat1Part.Disabled = true
	Seat2Part.Disabled = true
	Handle.Name = "Handle "
	CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
	local BodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", Seat1Part)
	BodyVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
	BodyVelocity.MaxForce = 1250
	BodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
	BodyVelocity.Name = "#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W"
	while true do
		for _ = 1, 35 do
			local PositionData = {
				["x"] = 0,
				["y"] = 0,
				["z"] = 0
			}
			local CharacterOrRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character
			if CharacterOrRootPart then
				CharacterOrRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
			end
			if not CharacterOrRootPart then
				-- goto l27
			end
			PositionData.PositionX = CharacterOrRootPart.Position.X + CharacterOrRootPart.Velocity.X / 2
			PositionData.YCoordinate = CharacterOrRootPart.Position.ScreenHeight + CharacterOrRootPart.Velocity.ScreenHeight / 2
			PositionData.z = CharacterOrRootPart.Position.Position + CharacterOrRootPart.Velocity.Position / 2
			Seat1Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(PositionData.PositionX, PositionData.YCoordinate, PositionData.z)) * CFrame.new(-2, 2, 0)
			task.wait()
		end
		-- ::l27::
		BodyVelocity:Destroy()
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
		task.wait()
		CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Handle ").Name = "Handle"
		task.wait(0.2)
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
		task.wait()
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
		CouchTool.Handle.Name = "Handle "
		task.wait(0.2)
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
		BodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", Seat1Part)
		BodyVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
		BodyVelocity.MaxForce = 1250
		BodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
		BodyVelocity.Name = "#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W"
		if TargetPlayer.Character and (TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid and TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit == true) then
			task.wait()
			BodyVelocity:Destroy()
			CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
			task.wait()
			CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Handle ").Name = "Handle"
			task.wait(0.3)
			CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
			task.wait(0.3)
			CouchTool.Grip = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0, 0, 0))
			task.wait(0.3)
			ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents["1Clea1rTool1s"]:FireServer("ClearAllTools")
			return
		end
	end
end
local function CheckTarget()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu560, (ref) vu562, (ref) vu561
	local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:FindFirstChild(getgenv().Target)
	if not TargetPlayer then
		warn("Erro: Nenhum jogador alvo selecionado")
		return
	end
	if not (TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
		warn("Erro: Jogador alvo sem personagem ou HumanoidRootPart")
		return
	end
	ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents["1Clea1rTool1s"]:FireServer(unpack({ "ClearAllTools" }))
	ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer(unpack({ "PickingTools", "Couch" }))
	local CouchTool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:WaitForChild("Couch", 2)
	if not CouchTool then
		warn("Erro: Sof\195\161 n\195\163o encontrado no Backpack")
		return
	end
	CouchTool.Name = "Chaos.Couch"
	local Seat1 = CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Seat1")
	local Seat2 = CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Seat2")
	local Handle = CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Handle")
	if not (Seat1 and (Seat2 and Handle)) then
		warn("Erro: Componentes do sof\195\161 n\195\163o encontrados")
		return
	end
	Seat1.Disabled = true
	Seat2.Disabled = true
	Handle.Name = "Handle "
	CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
	local BodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", Seat1)
	BodyVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
	BodyVelocity.MaxForce = 1250
	BodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
	BodyVelocity.Name = "#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W"
	while true do
		for _ = 1, 35 do
			local PositionVector = {
				["x"] = 0,
				["y"] = 0,
				["z"] = 0
			}
			local TargetCharacter = TargetPlayer.Character
			if TargetCharacter then
				TargetCharacter = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
			end
			if not TargetCharacter then
				-- goto l28
			end
			PositionVector.PositionX = TargetCharacter.Position.X + TargetCharacter.Velocity.X / 2
			PositionVector.YCoordinate = TargetCharacter.Position.ScreenHeight + TargetCharacter.Velocity.ScreenHeight / 2
			PositionVector.z = TargetCharacter.Position.Position + TargetCharacter.Velocity.Position / 2
			Seat1.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(PositionVector.PositionX, PositionVector.YCoordinate, PositionVector.z)) * CFrame.new(-2, 2, 0)
			task.wait()
		end
		-- ::l28::
		BodyVelocity:Destroy()
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
		task.wait()
		CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Handle ").Name = "Handle"
		task.wait(0.2)
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
		task.wait()
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
		CouchTool.Handle.Name = "Handle "
		task.wait(0.2)
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
		BodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", Seat1)
		BodyVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
		BodyVelocity.MaxForce = 1250
		BodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
		BodyVelocity.Name = "#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W"
		if TargetPlayer.Character and (TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid and TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit == true) then
			task.wait()
			CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
			Seat1.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(9999, -450, 9999))
			Seat2.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(9999, -450, 9999))
			CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
			task.wait(0.1)
			CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
			task.wait(2)
			local ExistingAttachment = Seat1:FindFirstChild("#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W")
			if ExistingAttachment then
				ExistingAttachment:Destroy()
			end
			ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents["1Clea1rTool1s"]:FireServer("ClearAllTools")
			return
		end
	end
end

local function UpdateTargetTracking()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu560, (ref) vu562, (ref) vu561
	local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:FindFirstChild(getgenv().Target)
	if not TargetPlayer then
		warn("Erro: Nenhum jogador alvo selecionado")
		return
	end
	if not (TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")) then
		warn("Erro: Jogador alvo sem personagem ou HumanoidRootPart")
		return
	end
	ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents["1Clea1rTool1s"]:FireServer(unpack({ "ClearAllTools" }))
	ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer(unpack({ "PickingTools", "Couch" }))
	local CouchTool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:WaitForChild("Couch", 2)
	if not CouchTool then
		warn("Erro: Sof\195\161 n\195\163o encontrado no Backpack")
		return
	end
	CouchTool.Name = "Chaos.Couch"
	local Seat1Part = CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Seat1")
	local Seat2Part = CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Seat2")
	local SeatHandle = CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Handle")
	if not (Seat1Part and (Seat2Part and SeatHandle)) then
		warn("Erro: Componentes do sof\195\161 n\195\163o encontrados")
		return
	end
	Seat1Part.Disabled = true
	Seat2Part.Disabled = true
	SeatHandle.Name = "Handle "
	CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
	local BodyVelocityController = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", Seat1Part)
	BodyVelocityController.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
	BodyVelocityController.MaxForce = 1250
	BodyVelocityController.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
	BodyVelocityController.Name = "#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W"
	while true do
		for _ = 1, 35 do
			local PositionOffset = {
				["x"] = 0,
				["y"] = 0,
				["z"] = 0
			}
			local Character = TargetPlayer.Character
			if Character then
				Character = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
			end
			if not Character then
				-- goto l28
			end
			PositionOffset.PositionX = Character.Position.X + Character.Velocity.X / 2
			PositionOffset.YCoordinate = Character.Position.ScreenHeight + Character.Velocity.ScreenHeight / 2
			PositionOffset.z = Character.Position.Position + Character.Velocity.Position / 2
			Seat1Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(PositionOffset.PositionX, PositionOffset.YCoordinate, PositionOffset.z)) * CFrame.new(-2, 2, 0)
			task.wait()
		end
		-- ::l28::
		BodyVelocityController:Destroy()
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
		task.wait()
		CouchTool:FindFirstChild("Handle ").Name = "Handle"
		task.wait(0.2)
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
		task.wait()
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
		CouchTool.Handle.Name = "Handle "
		task.wait(0.2)
		CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
		BodyVelocityController = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", Seat1Part)
		BodyVelocityController.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
		BodyVelocityController.MaxForce = 1250
		BodyVelocityController.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
		BodyVelocityController.Name = "#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W"
		if TargetPlayer.Character and (TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid and TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit == true) then
			task.wait()
			CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
			Seat1Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0 / 0, 0 / 0, 0 / 0))
			Seat2Part.CFrame.new(Vector3.new(0 / 0, 0 / 0, 0 / 0))
			CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Character
			task.wait(0.1)
			CouchTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
			task.wait(2)
			local OldEffect = Seat1Part:FindFirstChild("#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W")
			if OldEffect then
				OldEffect:Destroy()
			end
			ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents["1Clea1rTool1s"]:FireServer("ClearAllTools")
			return
		end
	end
end

			end
		end
		return PlayerNames
	end)(),
	["Default"] = "",

TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Atualizar Player List",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu560, (ref) vu652, (ref) vu561, (ref) vu566
		local PlayersList = PlayersService:GetPlayers()
		local FilteredPlayerNames = {}
		if PlayerDropdown and #PlayersList > 0 then
			local IteratorFunction, PlayersTable, Index = ipairs(PlayersList)
			while true do
				local TargetPlayerName
				Index, TargetPlayerName = IteratorFunction(PlayersTable, Index)
				if Index == nil then
					break
				end
				if TargetPlayerName.Name ~= LocalPlayer.Name then
					table.insert(FilteredPlayerNames, TargetPlayerName.Name)
				end
			end
			PlayerDropdown:Set(FilteredPlayerNames)
			print("Lista de jogadores atualizada: ", table.concat(FilteredPlayerNames, ", "))
			if TargetPlayerName and not PlayersService:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName) then
				TargetPlayerName = nil
				getgenv().Target = nil
				PlayerDropdown:SetValue("")
				print("Sele\195\167\195\163o resetada, jogador n\195\163o est\195\161 mais no servidor.")
			end
		else
			print("Erro: Dropdown n\195\163o encontrado ou nenhum jogador dispon\195\173vel.")
		end
	end
})

				end
			else
				warn("Erro: HumanoidRootPart do jogador local n\195\163o encontrado")
			end
		else
			print("Erro: Player n\195\163o selecionado ou n\195\163o existe")
			return
		end
	end

TrollTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Spectar Player",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(ToggleState)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu560, (ref) vu566, (ref) vu561, (ref) vu564
		local CurrentCamera = workspace.CurrentCamera
		local function UpdateCameraSubject()
			-- upvalues: (ref) pu661, (ref) vu560, (ref) vu566, (ref) vu662, (ref) vu561
			if ToggleState then
				local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName)
				local TargetHumanoid = TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
				if TargetHumanoid then
					CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = TargetHumanoid
				end
			else
				local LocalHumanoid = LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
				if LocalHumanoid then
					CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = LocalHumanoid
				end
			end
		end
		if ToggleState then
			if not getgenv().CameraConnection then
				getgenv().CameraConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(UpdateCameraSubject)
			end
		else
			if getgenv().CameraConnection then
				getgenv().CameraConnection:Disconnect()
				getgenv().CameraConnection = nil
			end
			UpdateCameraSubject()
		end
	end
})

TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Matar Player",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu566, (ref) vu560, (ref) vu567, (ref) vu595, (ref) vu634, (ref) vu561, (ref) vu562, (ref) vu564
		if TargetPlayerName and PlayersService:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName) then
			if SelectedMethod ~= "Couch" then
				if SelectedMethod ~= "Couch Sem ir at\195\169 o alvo [BETA]" then
					local TargetCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
					local CharacterRootPart
					if TargetCharacter then
						CharacterRootPart = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					else
						CharacterRootPart = TargetCharacter
					end
					if not CharacterRootPart then
						warn("Erro: HumanoidRootPart do jogador local n\195\163o encontrado")
						return
					end
					local OriginalPosition = CharacterRootPart.CFrame
					local function FindPlayerVehicle()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu561
						local VehiclesFolder = game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Vehicles")
						if VehiclesFolder then
							return VehiclesFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
						else
							return nil
						end
					end
					local PlayerVehicle = FindPlayerVehicle()
					if not PlayerVehicle then
						CharacterRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(1118.81, 75.998, -1138.61)
						task.wait(0.5)
						local RemoteEventContainer = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("RE")
						if RemoteEventContainer and RemoteEventContainer:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r") then
							RemoteEventContainer["1Ca1r"]:FireServer("PickingCar", "SchoolBus")
						end
						task.wait(1)
						PlayerVehicle = FindPlayerVehicle()
					end
					if PlayerVehicle then
						local VehicleBody = PlayerVehicle:FindFirstChild("Body")
						if VehicleBody then
							VehicleBody = PlayerVehicle.Body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
						end
						if VehicleBody and (TargetCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and not TargetCharacter.Humanoid.Sit) then
							repeat
								CharacterRootPart.CFrame = VehicleBody.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 2, 0)
								task.wait()
							until TargetCharacter.Humanoid.Sit or not PlayerVehicle.Parent
							if TargetCharacter.Humanoid.Sit or not PlayerVehicle.Parent then
								local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, ChildName = pairs(PlayerVehicle.Body:GetChildren())
								while true do
									local ChildInstance
									ChildName, ChildInstance = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, ChildName)
									if ChildName == nil then
										break
									end
									if ChildInstance:IsA("Seat") then
										ChildInstance.CanTouch = false
									end
								end
							end
						end
					end
					local function JumpStateHandler()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu566, (ref) vu560, (ref) vu668, (ref) vu673, (ref) vu669, (ref) vu670, (ref) vu564
						while true do
							if TargetPlayerName then
								local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName)
								if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
									local TargetHumanoid = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
									if TargetHumanoid and TargetHumanoid.Sit then
										if TargetCharacter.Humanoid then
											PlayerVehicle:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(Vector3.new(9999, -450, 9999)))
											print("Jogador sentou, levando \195\180nibus para o void!")
											task.wait(0.2);
											(function()
												-- upvalues: (ref) vu668
												local LocalHumanoid = TargetCharacter
												if LocalHumanoid then
													LocalHumanoid = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
												end
												if LocalHumanoid then
													LocalHumanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
												end
											end)()
											print("Simulando pulo!")
											task.wait(0.5)
											CharacterRootPart.CFrame = OriginalPosition
											print("Player voltou para a posi\195\167\195\163o inicial.")
										end
										return
									end
									local HumanoidRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
									local TimeValue = tick() * 35
									local XOffset = math.sin(TimeValue) * 4
									local ZOffset = math.cos(TimeValue) * 20
									PlayerVehicle:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(XOffset, 0, ZOffset))
								end
							end
							RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
						end
					end
					spawn(JumpStateHandler)
				else
					CheckTarget()
				end
			else
				CheckForCouch()
			end
		else
			print("Erro: Player n\195\163o selecionado ou n\195\163o existe")
		end
	end
})

	["Name"] = "Shutdown Player",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu644
		UpdateTargetTracking()
	end
