TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Puxar Player",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu566, (ref) vu560, (ref) vu567, (ref) vu615, (ref) vu624, (ref) vu561, (ref) vu562, (ref) vu564
		if TargetPlayerName and PlayersService:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName) then
			if SelectedMethod ~= "Couch" then
				if SelectedMethod ~= "Couch Sem ir at\195\169 o alvo [BETA]" then
					local TargetCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
					local HumanoidRootPart
					if TargetCharacter then
						HumanoidRootPart = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					else
						HumanoidRootPart = TargetCharacter
					end
					if not HumanoidRootPart then
						warn("Erro: HumanoidRootPart do jogador local n\195\163o encontrado")
						return
					end
					local TargetCFrame = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
					local function FindPlayerVehicle()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu561
						local VehiclesFolder = game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Vehicles")
						if VehiclesFolder then
							return VehiclesFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
						else
							return nil
						end
					end
					local PlayerVehicle = FindPlayerVehicle()
					if not PlayerVehicle then
						HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(1118.81, 75.998, -1138.61)
						task.wait(0.5)
						local RemoteEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("RE")
						if RemoteEvent and RemoteEvent:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r") then
							RemoteEvent["1Ca1r"]:FireServer("PickingCar", "SchoolBus")
						end
						task.wait(1)
						PlayerVehicle = FindPlayerVehicle()
					end
					if PlayerVehicle then
						local VehicleSeat = PlayerVehicle:FindFirstChild("Body")
						if VehicleSeat then
							VehicleSeat = PlayerVehicle.Body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
						end
						if VehicleSeat and (TargetCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and not TargetCharacter.Humanoid.Sit) then
							repeat
								HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 2, 0)
								task.wait()
							until TargetCharacter.Humanoid.Sit or not PlayerVehicle.Parent
						end
					end
					local function TeleportRoutine()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu566, (ref) vu560, (ref) vu688, (ref) vu693, (ref) vu690, (ref) vu562, (ref) vu564
						while true do
							if TargetPlayerName then
								local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName)
								if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
									local Humanoid = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
									if Humanoid and Humanoid.Sit then
										if TargetCharacter.Humanoid then
											PlayerVehicle:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(TargetCFrame)
											task.wait(0.7)
											ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer(unpack({ "DeleteAllVehicles" }))
										end
										return
									end
									local HumanoidRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
									local TimeValue = tick() * 35
									local SineOffset = math.sin(TimeValue) * 4
									local CosineOffset = math.cos(TimeValue) * 20
									PlayerVehicle:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(SineOffset, 0, CosineOffset))
								end
							end
							RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
						end
					end
					spawn(TeleportRoutine)
				else
					UpdateParticle()
				end
			else
				HandleSitAnimation()
			end
		else
			print("Erro: Player n\195\163o selecionado ou n\195\163o existe")
		end
	end
})
TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "House Ban Kill",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu566
		if not TargetPlayerName then
			print("Nenhum jogador selecionado!")
			return
		end
		local LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
		local _ = LocalPlayer.Backpack
		local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
		local CharacterRef = Character
		local Humanoid = Character.FindFirstChildOfClass(CharacterRef, "Humanoid")
		local LocalPlayer = Character
		local HumanoidRootPart = Character.FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer, "HumanoidRootPart")
		local WorkspaceLots = game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("001_Lots")
		local _ = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
		local RotationAngle = 0
		local VehiclesFolder = Workspace.Vehicles
		function Check()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu703, (ref) vu704, (ref) vu706, (ref) vu708, (ref) vu711
			return LocalPlayer and (Character and (Humanoid and (HumanoidRootPart and VehiclesFolder))) and true or false
		end
		local TargetPlayer = game.Players:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName)
		if TargetPlayer and (TargetPlayer.Character and Check()) then
			if not WorkspaceLots:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "House") then
				local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, CurrentIndex = pairs(WorkspaceLots:GetChildren())
				local AvailableLots = {}
				while true do
					local CurrentChild
					CurrentIndex, CurrentChild = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, CurrentIndex)
					if CurrentIndex == nil then
						break
					end
					if CurrentChild.Name == "For Sale" then
						local IteratorFunction, TableState, CurrentKey = pairs(CurrentChild:GetDescendants())
						while true do
							local CurrentValue
							CurrentKey, CurrentValue = IteratorFunction(TableState, CurrentKey)
							if CurrentKey == nil then
								break
							end
							if CurrentValue:IsA("NumberValue") and (CurrentValue.Name == "Number" and (CurrentValue.Value < 25 and CurrentValue.Value > 10)) then
								table.insert(AvailableLots, {
									["Lot"] = CurrentChild,
									["Number"] = CurrentValue.Value
								})
								break
							end
						end
					end
				end
				if #AvailableLots <= 0 then
					print("Nenhuma casa dispon\195\131\194\173vel para compra!")
					return
				end
				local SelectedLotData = AvailableLots[math.random(1, #AvailableLots)]
				local LotInstance = SelectedLotData.Lot
				local LotNumber = SelectedLotData.Number
				local BuyHousePart = LotInstance:FindFirstChild("BuyHouse")
				local _ = BuyHousePart.Position
				if BuyHousePart and BuyHousePart:IsA("BasePart") then
					HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = BuyHousePart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, -6, 0)
					task.wait(0.5)
					local ClickDetector = BuyHousePart:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector")
					if ClickDetector then
						fireclickdetector(ClickDetector)
					end
				end
				task.wait(0.5)
				game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("Remotes"):WaitForChild("Lot:BuildProperty"):FireServer(unpack({ LotNumber, "056_House" }))
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
			local PlayerHouse = WorkspaceLots:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "House")
			if PlayerHouse then
				task.wait(0.5)
				local DescendantIterator, DescendantTable, DescendantIndex = pairs(PlayerHouse:GetDescendants())
				local NumberValueInstance = nil
				while true do
					local CurrentDescendant
					DescendantIndex, CurrentDescendant = DescendantIterator(DescendantTable, DescendantIndex)
					if DescendantIndex == nil then
						break
					end
					if CurrentDescendant.Name == "Number" then
						if CurrentDescendant:IsA("NumberValue") then
							NumberValueInstance = CurrentDescendant
						end
					end
				end
				task.wait(0.5)
				game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Gettin1gHous1e"):FireServer("PickingCustomHouse", "049_House", NumberValueInstance.Value)
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
			local VehicleFolder = VehiclesFolder
			if not VehiclesFolder.FindFirstChild(VehicleFolder, LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car") and Check() then
				HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(1118.81, 75.998, -1138.61)
				task.wait(0.5)
				game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer("PickingCar", "SchoolBus")
				task.wait(0.5)
				local PlayerCar = VehiclesFolder
				local CarModel = VehiclesFolder.FindFirstChild(PlayerCar, LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
				task.wait(0.5)
				local VehicleSeat = CarModel:FindFirstChild("Body")
				if VehicleSeat then
					VehicleSeat = CarModel.Body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
				end
				if VehicleSeat then
					repeat
						task.wait()
						HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, math.random(-1, 1), 0)
					until Humanoid.Sit
				end
			end
			task.wait(0.5)
			local PlayerCar = VehiclesFolder
			local CarModel = VehiclesFolder.FindFirstChild(PlayerCar, LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
			if CarModel then
				if not Humanoid.Sit then
					local VehicleSeat = CarModel:FindFirstChild("Body")
					if VehicleSeat then
						VehicleSeat = CarModel.Body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
					end
					if VehicleSeat then
						repeat
							task.wait()
							HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, math.random(-1, 1), 0)
						until Humanoid.Sit
					end
				end
				local Character = TargetPlayer.Character
				local Humanoid = Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
				local HumanoidRootPart = Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if Character and (Humanoid and (HumanoidRootPart and not Humanoid.Sit)) then
					while not Humanoid.Sit do
						task.wait()
						local function SetPrimaryPartCFrameFunction(PositionCFrame, RotationOffset, PositionOffset)
							-- upvalues: (ref) vu738
							CarModel:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(PositionCFrame.Position) * RotationOffset * PositionOffset)
						end
						RotationAngle = RotationAngle + 100
						SetPrimaryPartCFrameFunction(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
						SetPrimaryPartCFrameFunction(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
						SetPrimaryPartCFrameFunction(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(2.25, 1.5, -2.25) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
						SetPrimaryPartCFrameFunction(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(-2.25, -1.5, 2.25) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
						SetPrimaryPartCFrameFunction(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
						SetPrimaryPartCFrameFunction(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
					end
					task.wait(0.2)
					local PlayerHouse = WorkspaceLots:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "House")
					CarModel:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(PlayerHouse.HouseSpawnPosition.Position))
					task.wait(0.2)
					local PlayerRegion = Region3.new(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - Vector3.new(30, 30, 30), game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position + Vector3.new(30, 30, 30))
					local RegionParts = workspace:FindPartsInRegion3(PlayerRegion, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart, math.huge)
					local PartsIterator, CurrentKey, NextKey = pairs(RegionParts)
					while true do
						local CurrentValue
						NextKey, CurrentValue = PartsIterator(CurrentKey, NextKey)
						if NextKey == nil then
							break
						end
						if CurrentValue.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then
							local BanArguments = { "BanPlayerFromHouse", game:GetService("Players"):FindFirstChild(CurrentValue.Parent.Name), CurrentValue.Parent }
							game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Playe1rTrigge1rEven1t"):FireServer(unpack(BanArguments))
							game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer(unpack({ "DeleteAllVehicles" }))
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end
	end
})
local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
local CurrentCamera = workspace.CurrentCamera
local IsToggleEnabled = false
TrollTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Auto Fling ",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(ToggleState)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu758, (ref) vu566, (ref) vu755, (ref) vu756, (ref) vu757
		IsToggleEnabled = ToggleState
		if ToggleState and TargetPlayerName then
			local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName)
			if not (TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character) then
				return
			end
			local CharacterOrRootPart = LocalPlayer.Character
			if CharacterOrRootPart then
				CharacterOrRootPart = LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			end
			local CharacterOrRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character
			if CharacterOrRootPart then
				CharacterOrRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			end
			if not (CharacterOrRootPart and CharacterOrRootPart) then
				return
			end
			local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
			local Humanoid = Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			local TargetCFrame = CharacterOrRootPart.CFrame
			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Clea1rTool1s"):FireServer(unpack({ "ClearAllTools" }))
			task.wait(0.2)
			local ToolNames = { "PickingTools", "Couch" }
			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer(unpack(ToolNames))
			task.wait(0.3)
			local CouchTool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Couch")
			if CouchTool then
				CouchTool.Parent = Character
			end
			task.wait(0.2)
			game:GetService("VirtualInputManager"):SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode.FKey, false, game)
			task.wait(0.25)
			workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = 0 / 0
			local FlingVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
			FlingVelocity.Name = "FlingForce"
			FlingVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
			FlingVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(1 / 0, 1 / 0, 1 / 0)
			FlingVelocity.Parent = CharacterOrRootPart
			Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, false)
			Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
			CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or (CharacterOrRootPart or Humanoid)
			task.spawn(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu761, (ref) vu758, (ref) vu760, (ref) vu768, (ref) vu764, (ref) vu765, (ref) vu757, (ref) vu763, (ref) vu766
				local ToolList = { CharacterOrRootPart }
				local ParticleUpdateCounter = 0
				while IsToggleEnabled and (TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character) and (TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and not TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid").Sit) do
					ParticleUpdateCounter = ParticleUpdateCounter + 50
					local IteratorFunction, ParticleTable, ParticleIndex = ipairs(ToolList)
					while true do
						local ParticleData
						ParticleIndex, ParticleData = IteratorFunction(ParticleTable, ParticleIndex)
						if ParticleIndex == nil then
							break
						end
						local PositionX = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.X
						local PositionY = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.ScreenHeight
						local PositionZ = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Position
						local PredictedPositionX = PositionX + TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.X / 1.5
						local PredictedPositionY = PositionY + TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.ScreenHeight / 1.5
						local PredictedPositionZ = PositionZ + TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Position / 1.5
						CharacterOrRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(PredictedPositionX, PredictedPositionY, PredictedPositionZ) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(ParticleUpdateCounter), 0, 0)
					end
					CharacterOrRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
					CharacterOrRootPart.RotVelocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
					task.wait()
				end
				IsToggleEnabled = false
				FlingVelocity:Destroy()
				Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true)
				Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
				CharacterOrRootPart.CFrame = TargetCFrame
				CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = Humanoid
				local DescendantsIterator = Character
				local NextFunction, DescendantsTable, CurrentIndex = pairs(DescendantsIterator:GetDescendants())
				while true do
					local CurrentDescendant
					CurrentIndex, CurrentDescendant = NextFunction(DescendantsTable, CurrentIndex)
					if CurrentIndex == nil then
						break
					end
					if CurrentDescendant:IsA("BasePart") then
						CurrentDescendant.Velocity = Vector3.zero
						CurrentDescendant.RotVelocity = Vector3.zero
					end
				end
				Humanoid:UnequipTools()
				game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer(unpack(ToolNames))
			end)
		end
	end
})
local function PlayerSetupFunction(Player)
	local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
	local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
	local Character = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
	local Character = Character
	local Humanoid = Character.WaitForChild(Character, "Humanoid")
	local Character = Character
	Character.WaitForChild(Character, "HumanoidRootPart")
	local Backpack = LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack")
	local SoccerBallsFolder = workspace.WorkspaceCom:WaitForChild("001_SoccerBalls")
	local function FindOrCreateSoccerBall()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu793, (ref) vu789, (ref) vu794, (ref) vu788
		if not Backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall") then
			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "SoccerBall")
		end
		repeat
			task.wait()
		until Backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall")
		Backpack.SoccerBall.Parent = Character
		repeat
			task.wait()
		until SoccerBallsFolder:FindFirstChild("Soccer" .. LocalPlayer.Name)
		Character.SoccerBall.Parent = Backpack
		return SoccerBallsFolder:FindFirstChild("Soccer" .. LocalPlayer.Name)
	end
	local SoccerBallsFolderRef = SoccerBallsFolder
	local SoccerBallInstance = SoccerBallsFolder.FindFirstChild(SoccerBallsFolderRef, "Soccer" .. LocalPlayer.Name) or FindOrCreateSoccerBall()
	SoccerBallInstance.CanCollide = false
	SoccerBallInstance.Massless = true
	SoccerBallInstance.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.new(0.0001, 0, 0)
	if Player == LocalPlayer then
		-- ::l9::
		return
	else
		local PlayerCharacter = Player.Character
		if not (PlayerCharacter and (PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("Humanoid"))) then
			-- goto l9
		end
		local HumanoidRootPart = PlayerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart
		local Humanoid = PlayerCharacter.Humanoid
		if SoccerBallInstance:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BodyVelocity") then
			SoccerBallInstance:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BodyVelocity"):Destroy()
		end
		local BodyVelocityInstance = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
		BodyVelocityInstance.Name = "FlingPower"
		BodyVelocityInstance.Velocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
		BodyVelocityInstance.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
		BodyVelocityInstance.MaxForce = math.huge
		BodyVelocityInstance.Parent = SoccerBallInstance
		workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = Humanoid
		os.time()
		while true do
			if true then
				if HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude <= 0 then
					local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, ChildIndex = pairs(PlayerCharacter:GetChildren())
					while true do
						local CurrentChild
						ChildIndex, CurrentChild = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, ChildIndex)
						if ChildIndex == nil then
							break
						end
						if CurrentChild:IsA("BasePart") and (CurrentChild.CanCollide and not CurrentChild.Anchored) then
							SoccerBallInstance.CFrame = CurrentChild.CFrame
							task.wait(0.00016666666666666666)
						end
					end
				else
					local PositionX = HumanoidRootPart.Position.X + HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.X / 1.5
					local PositionY = HumanoidRootPart.Position.ScreenHeight + HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.ScreenHeight / 1.5
					local PositionZ = HumanoidRootPart.Position.Position + HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Position / 1.5
					local VectorPosition = Vector3.new(PositionX, PositionY, PositionZ)
					SoccerBallInstance.CFrame = CFrame.new(VectorPosition)
					SoccerBallInstance.Orientation = SoccerBallInstance.Orientation + Vector3.new(45, 60, 30)
				end
			end
			task.wait(0.00016666666666666666)
			if HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude > 1000 or (Humanoid.Health <= 0 or (not PlayerCharacter:IsDescendantOf(workspace) or Player.Parent ~= PlayersService)) then
				workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = Humanoid
				-- goto l9
			end
		end
	end
end
TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Fling Ball",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu810, (ref) vu566
		PlayerSetupFunction(game:GetService("Players")[TargetPlayerName])
	end

local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
local function _(ItemName)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu811
	local IteratorFunction, BackpackItems, CurrentItem = pairs(LocalPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren())
	while true do
		local ItemName
		CurrentItem, ItemName = IteratorFunction(BackpackItems, CurrentItem)
		if CurrentItem == nil then
			break
		end
		if ItemName.Name == ItemName then
			return true
		end
	end
	return false
end
local function _(ToolName)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu811
	local FoundTool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild(ToolName)
	if FoundTool then
		LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(FoundTool)
	end
end
local function _(ToolToUnequip)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu811
	local FoundCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild(ToolToUnequip)
	if FoundCharacter then
		FoundCharacter.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
	end
end

TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Fling - Boat",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu566
		if TargetPlayerName and game.Players:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName) then
			local LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
			local PlayerCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
			local Humanoid
			if PlayerCharacter then
				Humanoid = PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			else
				Humanoid = PlayerCharacter
			end
			if PlayerCharacter then
				PlayerCharacter = PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			end
			local VehiclesFolder = game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Vehicles")
			if Humanoid and PlayerCharacter then
				local PlayerVehicle = VehiclesFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car") or (function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) vu822, (ref) vu824, (ref) vu821
					PlayerCharacter.CFrame = CFrame.new(1754, -2, 58)
					task.wait(0.5)
					game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer("PickingBoat", "MilitaryBoatFree")
					task.wait(1)
					return VehiclesFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
				end)()
				if PlayerVehicle then
					local VehicleBody = PlayerVehicle:FindFirstChild("Body")
					if VehicleBody then
						VehicleBody = PlayerVehicle.Body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
					end
					if VehicleBody then
						repeat
							task.wait(0.1)
							PlayerCharacter.CFrame = VehicleBody.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0)
						until Humanoid.SeatPart == VehicleBody
						print("Barco spawnado!")
						local TargetPlayer = game.Players:FindFirstChild(TargetPlayerName)
						if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character then
							local TargetCharacter = TargetPlayer.Character
							local TargetHumanoid = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
							local HumanoidRootPart = TargetCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
							if HumanoidRootPart and TargetHumanoid then
								local SpinningVelocity = Instance.new("BodyAngularVelocity")
								SpinningVelocity.Name = "Spinning"
								SpinningVelocity.Parent = PlayerVehicle.PrimaryPart
								SpinningVelocity.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(0, math.huge, 0)
								SpinningVelocity.AngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 369, 0)
								print("Fling ativo!")
								local function ApplyCharacterOffset(Character, OffsetVector)
									-- upvalues: (ref) vu825
									if PlayerVehicle and PlayerVehicle.PrimaryPart then
										PlayerVehicle:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(Character.Position + OffsetVector))
									end
								end
								task.spawn(function()
									-- upvalues: (ref) vu825, (ref) vu830, (ref) vu834, (ref) vu831
									while PlayerVehicle and (PlayerVehicle.Parent and (HumanoidRootPart and HumanoidRootPart.Parent)) do
										task.wait(0.01)
										ApplyCharacterOffset(HumanoidRootPart, Vector3.new(0, 1, 0))
										ApplyCharacterOffset(HumanoidRootPart, Vector3.new(0, -2.25, 5))
										ApplyCharacterOffset(HumanoidRootPart, Vector3.new(0, 2.25, 0.25))
										ApplyCharacterOffset(HumanoidRootPart, Vector3.new(-2.25, -1.5, 2.25))
										ApplyCharacterOffset(HumanoidRootPart, Vector3.new(0, 1.5, 0))
										ApplyCharacterOffset(HumanoidRootPart, Vector3.new(0, -1.5, 0))
										if PlayerVehicle and PlayerVehicle.PrimaryPart then
											local RandomRotation = CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-369, 369)), math.rad(math.random(-369, 369)), math.rad(math.random(-369, 369)))
											PlayerVehicle:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(HumanoidRootPart.Position + Vector3.new(0, 1.5, 0)) * RandomRotation)
										end
									end
									if SpinningVelocity and SpinningVelocity.Parent then
										SpinningVelocity:Destroy()
										print("Fling desativado")
									end
								end)
							else
								warn("Humanoid ou RootPart do alvo n\195\163o encontrado")
							end
						else
							warn("Jogador n\195\163o encontrado")
							return
						end
					else
						warn("Assento n\195\163o encontrado")
						return
					end
				else
					warn("Falha ao spawnar o barco")
					return
				end
			else
				warn("Humanoid ou RootPart inv\195\161lido")
				return
			end
		else
			warn("Nenhum jogador selecionado ou n\195\163o existe")
			return
		end
	end
})

TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Desligar Fling - Boat",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
		local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
		local HumanoidRootPart
		if Character then
			HumanoidRootPart = Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		else
			HumanoidRootPart = Character
		end
		if Character then
			Character = Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		end
		local PlayerVehicle = game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Vehicles")
		if HumanoidRootPart and Character then
			Character.PlatformStand = true
			print("Jogador paralisado para reduzir efeitos do spin.")
			local ChildIterator, CurrentChild, ChildIndex = pairs(HumanoidRootPart:GetChildren())
			while true do
				local ChildInstance
				ChildIndex, ChildInstance = ChildIterator(CurrentChild, ChildIndex)
				if ChildIndex == nil then
					break
				end
				if ChildInstance:IsA("BodyAngularVelocity") or ChildInstance:IsA("BodyVelocity") then
					ChildInstance:Destroy()
				end
			end
			print("Spin e for\195\167as removidas do jogador.")
			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer("DeleteAllVehicles")
			task.wait(0.5)
			if PlayerVehicle then
				PlayerVehicle = PlayerVehicle:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
			end
			if PlayerVehicle and PlayerVehicle.PrimaryPart then
				local PrimaryPartIterator, PrimaryPartCurrentChild, ChildName = pairs(PlayerVehicle.PrimaryPart:GetChildren())
				while true do
					local ChildInstance
					ChildName, ChildInstance = PrimaryPartIterator(PrimaryPartCurrentChild, ChildName)
					if ChildName == nil then
						break
					end
					if ChildInstance:IsA("BodyAngularVelocity") or ChildInstance:IsA("BodyVelocity") then
						ChildInstance:Destroy()
					end
				end
				print("Spin removido do barco.")
			end
			task.wait(1)
			local TargetPosition = Vector3.new(0, 1000, 0)
			local BodyPositionInstance = Instance.new("BodyPosition", HumanoidRootPart)
			BodyPositionInstance.Position = TargetPosition
			BodyPositionInstance.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
			local BodyGyro = Instance.new("BodyGyro", HumanoidRootPart)
			BodyGyro.CFrame = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
			BodyGyro.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
			print("Jogador est\195\161 preso na coordenada segura.")
			task.wait(3)
			BodyPositionInstance:Destroy()
			BodyGyro:Destroy()
			Character.PlatformStand = false
			print("Jogador liberado, seguro na posi\195\167\195\163o.")
		else
			warn("Nenhum RootPart ou Humanoid encontrado!")
		end
	end
})
TrollTab:AddSection({

TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Click Fling Portas [Beta]",
	["Description"] = "Para Usar, Recomendo chegar perto de outras portas, apos ela ir at\195\169 voc\195\170, clique no jogador que deseja flingar",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
		local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
		local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
		local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
		local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
		local HumanoidRootPart = (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()):WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local TeleportPart = Instance.new("Part")
		TeleportPart.Size = Vector3.new(100000, 100000, 100000)
		TeleportPart.Transparency = 1
		TeleportPart.Anchored = true
		TeleportPart.CanCollide = false
		TeleportPart.Name = "BlackHoleTarget"
		TeleportPart.Parent = Workspace
		local BlackHoleAttachment = Instance.new("Attachment")
		BlackHoleAttachment.Name = "Luscaa_BlackHoleAttachment"
		BlackHoleAttachment.Parent = TeleportPart
		RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu857, (ref) vu856
			TeleportPart.CFrame = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
		end)
		local AffectedParts = {}
		local function ProcessDoorPart(TargetPart)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu858, (ref) vu859
			if TargetPart:IsA("BasePart") and (not TargetPart.Anchored and string.find(TargetPart.Name, "Door")) then
				if not TargetPart:FindFirstChild("Luscaa_Attached") then
					TargetPart.CanCollide = false
					local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, Index = ipairs(TargetPart:GetChildren())
					while true do
						local ChildInstance
						Index, ChildInstance = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, Index)
						if Index == nil then
							break
						end
						if ChildInstance:IsA("AlignPosition") or (ChildInstance:IsA("Torque") or ChildInstance:IsA("Attachment")) then
							ChildInstance:Destroy()
						end
					end
					Instance.new("BoolValue", TargetPart).Name = "Luscaa_Attached"
					local AttachmentInstance = Instance.new("Attachment", TargetPart)
					local AlignPosition = Instance.new("AlignPosition", TargetPart)
					AlignPosition.Attachment0 = AttachmentInstance
					AlignPosition.Attachment1 = BlackHoleAttachment
					AlignPosition.MaxForce = 1e20
					AlignPosition.MaxVelocity = math.huge
					AlignPosition.Responsiveness = 99999
					local Torque = Instance.new("Torque", TargetPart)
					Torque.Attachment0 = AttachmentInstance
					Torque.RelativeTo = Enum.ActuatorRelativeTo.World
					Torque.Torque = Vector3.new(math.random(-1000000, 1000000) * 10000, math.random(-1000000, 1000000) * 10000, math.random(-1000000, 1000000) * 10000)
					table.insert(AffectedParts, {
						["Part"] = TargetPart,
						["Align"] = AlignPosition
					})
				end
			else
				return
			end
		end
		local Iterator, Table, Index = ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants())
		local TargetAttachment = BlackHoleAttachment
		local DoorParts = AffectedParts
		while true do
			local Descendant
			Index, Descendant = Iterator(Table, Index)
			if Index == nil then
				break
			end
			if Descendant:IsA("BasePart") and string.find(Descendant.Name, "Door") then
				ProcessDoorPart(Descendant)
			end
		end
		Workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(AddedDescendant)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu868
			if AddedDescendant:IsA("BasePart") and string.find(AddedDescendant.Name, "Door") then
				ProcessDoorPart(AddedDescendant)
			end
		end)
		local function HandlePlayerAttachment(Player)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu873, (ref) vu853, (ref) vu872
			local Character = Player.Character
			if Character then
				local HumanoidRootPart = Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if HumanoidRootPart then
					local TargetAttachment = HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("SHNMAX_TargetAttachment")
					if not TargetAttachment then
						TargetAttachment = Instance.new("Attachment", HumanoidRootPart)
						TargetAttachment.Name = "SHNMAX_TargetAttachment"
					end
					local IteratorFunction, Index, Value = ipairs(DoorParts)
					while true do
						local Particle
						Value, Particle = IteratorFunction(Index, Value)
						if Value == nil then
							break
						end
						if Particle.Align then
							Particle.Align.Attachment1 = TargetAttachment
						end
					end
					local StartTime = tick()
					while tick() - StartTime < 5 and HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude < 20 do
						RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
					end
					local IteratorFunction, Index, Index = ipairs(DoorParts)
					while true do
						local Particle
						Index, Particle = IteratorFunction(Index, Index)
						if Index == nil then
							break
						end
						if Particle.Align then
							Particle.Align.Attachment1 = TargetAttachment
						end
					end
				end
			else
				return
			end
		end
		UserInputService.TouchTap:Connect(function(TouchPositions, IsGameProcessed)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu852, (ref) vu851, (ref) vu855, (ref) vu889
			if not IsGameProcessed then
				local FirstTouchPosition = TouchPositions[1]
				local ScreenRay = Workspace.CurrentCamera:ScreenPointToRay(FirstTouchPosition.X, FirstTouchPosition.ScreenHeight)
				local RaycastResult = Workspace:Raycast(ScreenRay.Origin, ScreenRay.Direction * 1000)
				if RaycastResult and RaycastResult.Instance then
					local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:GetPlayerFromCharacter(RaycastResult.Instance:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model"))
					if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer ~= LocalPlayer then
						HandlePlayerAttachment(TargetPlayer)
					end
				end
			end
		end)
	end
})

	["Name"] = "Click Fling Admin [Beta]",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local Players = game:GetService("Players")

		local AffectedDoors = {}
		local function ProcessDoorPart(DoorPart)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu903, (ref) vu904
			if DoorPart:IsA("BasePart") and (not DoorPart.Anchored and string.find(DoorPart.Name, "Door")) then
				if not DoorPart:FindFirstChild("Luscaa_Attached") then
					DoorPart.CanCollide = false
					DoorPart.Transparency = 1
					local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, ChildIndex = ipairs(DoorPart:GetChildren())
					while true do
						local ChildInstance
						ChildIndex, ChildInstance = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, ChildIndex)
						if ChildIndex == nil then
							break
						end
						if ChildInstance:IsA("AlignPosition") or (ChildInstance:IsA("Torque") or ChildInstance:IsA("Attachment")) then
							ChildInstance:Destroy()
						end
					end
					Instance.new("BoolValue", DoorPart).Name = "Luscaa_Attached"
					local AttachmentInstance = Instance.new("Attachment", DoorPart)
					local AlignPosition = Instance.new("AlignPosition", DoorPart)
					AlignPosition.Attachment0 = AttachmentInstance
					AlignPosition.Attachment1 = BlackHoleAttachment
					AlignPosition.MaxForce = 1e20
					AlignPosition.MaxVelocity = math.huge
					AlignPosition.Responsiveness = 99999
					local Torque = Instance.new("Torque", DoorPart)
					Torque.Attachment0 = AttachmentInstance
					Torque.RelativeTo = Enum.ActuatorRelativeTo.World
					Torque.Torque = Vector3.new(math.random(-1000000, 1000000) * 10000, math.random(-1000000, 1000000) * 10000, math.random(-1000000, 1000000) * 10000)
					table.insert(AffectedDoors, {
						["Part"] = DoorPart,
						["Align"] = AlignPosition
					})
				end
			else
				return
			end
		end
		local IndexIterator, DescendantsList, CurrentIndex = ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants())
		local DoorAttachment = BlackHoleAttachment
		local DoorParts = AffectedDoors
		while true do
			local Descendant
			CurrentIndex, Descendant = IndexIterator(DescendantsList, CurrentIndex)
			if CurrentIndex == nil then
				break
			end
			if Descendant:IsA("BasePart") and string.find(Descendant.Name, "Door") then
				ProcessDoorPart(Descendant)
			end
		end
		Workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(NewDescendant)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu913
			if NewDescendant:IsA("BasePart") and string.find(NewDescendant.Name, "Door") then
				ProcessDoorPart(NewDescendant)
			end
		end)
		local function ProcessDoor(Player)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu918, (ref) vu898, (ref) vu917
			local Character = Player.Character
			if Character then
				local HumanoidRootPart = Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if HumanoidRootPart then
					local TargetAttachment = HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("SHNMAX_TargetAttachment")
					if not TargetAttachment then
						TargetAttachment = Instance.new("Attachment", HumanoidRootPart)
						TargetAttachment.Name = "SHNMAX_TargetAttachment"
					end
					local IteratorFunction, ParticleArray, Index = ipairs(DoorParts)
					while true do
						local Particle
						Index, Particle = IteratorFunction(ParticleArray, Index)
						if Index == nil then
							break
						end
						if Particle.Align then
							Particle.Align.Attachment1 = TargetAttachment
						end
					end
					local StartTime = tick()
					while tick() - StartTime < 5 and HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude < 20 do
						RunService.Heartbeat:Wait()
					end
					local IteratorFunction, ParticleArray, Index = ipairs(DoorParts)
					while true do
						local Particle
						Index, Particle = IteratorFunction(ParticleArray, Index)
						if Index == nil then
							break
						end
						if Particle.Align then
							Particle.Align.Attachment1 = DoorAttachment
						end
					end
				end
			else
				return
			end
		end
		UserInputService.TouchTap:Connect(function(TouchPositions, IsGameProcessed)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu897, (ref) vu896, (ref) vu900, (ref) vu934
			if not IsGameProcessed then
				local FirstTouchPosition = TouchPositions[1]
				local ScreenRay = Workspace.CurrentCamera:ScreenPointToRay(FirstTouchPosition.X, FirstTouchPosition.ScreenHeight)
				local RaycastResult = Workspace:Raycast(ScreenRay.Origin, ScreenRay.Direction * 1000)
				if RaycastResult and RaycastResult.Instance then
					local TargetPlayer = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(RaycastResult.Instance:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model"))
					if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer ~= LocalPlayer then
						ProcessDoor(TargetPlayer)
					end
				end
			end
		end)
	end
})
TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Click Fling Couch (Tool)",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
		local ReplicatedStorageService = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
		local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
		local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
		local CurrentCamera = workspace.CurrentCamera
		local IsFlingEnabled = true
		local IsFlingingEnabled = false
		local ToolName = "Click Fling Couch"
		local PlayerBackpack = LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack")
		if not (PlayerBackpack:FindFirstChild(ToolName) or LocalPlayer.Character and LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild(ToolName)) then
			local FlingTool = Instance.new("Tool")
			FlingTool.Name = ToolName
			FlingTool.RequiresHandle = false
			FlingTool.CanBeDropped = false
			FlingTool.Equipped:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu947
				IsFlingingEnabled = true
			end)
			FlingTool.Unequipped:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu947
				IsFlingingEnabled = false
			end)
			FlingTool.Parent = PlayerBackpack
		end
		local function HandlePlayerTarget(TargetPlayer)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu947, (ref) vu944, (ref) vu942, (ref) vu945
			if IsFlingingEnabled then
				if TargetPlayer and (TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer ~= LocalPlayer) then
					local IsTargeting = true
					local CharacterRootPart = LocalPlayer.Character
					if CharacterRootPart then
						CharacterRootPart = LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					end
					local CharacterRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character
					if CharacterRootPart then
						CharacterRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					end
					if CharacterRootPart and CharacterRootPart then
						local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
						local Humanoid = Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
						local OriginalCFrame = CharacterRootPart.CFrame
						ReplicatedStorageService:WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Clea1rTool1s"):FireServer("ClearAllTools")
						task.wait(0.2)
						ReplicatedStorageService.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "Couch")
						task.wait(0.3)
						local CouchTool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Couch")
						if CouchTool then
							CouchTool.Parent = Character
						end
						task.wait(0.1)
						game:GetService("VirtualInputManager"):SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode.FKey, false, game)
						task.wait(0.25)
						workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = 0 / 0
						local ThrowForce = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
						ThrowForce.Name = "ForcaJogada"
						ThrowForce.Velocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
						ThrowForce.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
						ThrowForce.Parent = CharacterRootPart
						Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, false)
						Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
						CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or (CharacterRootPart or Humanoid)
						task.spawn(function()
							-- upvalues: (ref) vu953, (ref) vu952, (ref) pu951, (ref) vu959, (ref) vu956, (ref) vu957, (ref) vu945, (ref) vu955, (ref) vu942
							local ParticleList = { CharacterRootPart }
							local RotationAngle = 0
							while IsTargeting and (TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character) and (TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and not TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid").Sit) do
								RotationAngle = RotationAngle + 50
								local IteratorFunction, ParticleList, Index = ipairs(ParticleList)
								while true do
									local NextKey
									Index, NextKey = IteratorFunction(ParticleList, Index)
									if Index == nil then
										break
									end
									local HumanoidRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
									local PredictedPosition = HumanoidRootPart.Position + HumanoidRootPart.Velocity / 1.5
									CharacterRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(PredictedPosition) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0)
								end
								CharacterRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
								CharacterRootPart.RotVelocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
								task.wait()
							end
							IsTargeting = false
							ThrowForce:Destroy()
							Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true)
							Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
							CharacterRootPart.CFrame = OriginalCFrame
							CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = Humanoid
							local CharacterModel = Character
							local DescendantsIterator, DescendantsTable, CurrentDescendant = pairs(CharacterModel:GetDescendants())
							while true do
								local DescendantInstance
								CurrentDescendant, DescendantInstance = DescendantsIterator(DescendantsTable, CurrentDescendant)
								if CurrentDescendant == nil then
									break
								end
								if DescendantInstance:IsA("BasePart") then
									DescendantInstance.Velocity = Vector3.zero
									DescendantInstance.RotVelocity = Vector3.zero
								end
							end
							Humanoid:UnequipTools()
							ReplicatedStorageService.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "Couch")
						end)
						while IsTargeting do
							task.wait()
						end
					end
				else
					return
				end
			else
				return
			end
		end
		UserInputService.TouchTap:Connect(function(TouchInputs, IsGameProcessed)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu946, (ref) vu947, (ref) vu945, (ref) vu941, (ref) vu944, (ref) vu973
			if not IsGameProcessed and (IsFlingEnabled and IsFlingingEnabled) then
				local ScreenPosition = TouchInputs[1]
				local MouseRay = CurrentCamera:ScreenPointToRay(ScreenPosition.X, ScreenPosition.ScreenHeight)
				local RaycastResult = workspace:Raycast(MouseRay.Origin, MouseRay.Direction * 1000)
				if RaycastResult and RaycastResult.Instance then
					local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:GetPlayerFromCharacter(RaycastResult.Instance:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model"))
					if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer ~= LocalPlayer then
						IsFlingEnabled = false
						HandlePlayerTarget(TargetPlayer)
						task.delay(2, function()
							-- upvalues: (ref) vu946
							IsFlingEnabled = true
						end)
					end
				end
			end
		end)
	end
})
TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Click Fling Ball (Tool)",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
		local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
		local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
		local CurrentCamera = Workspace.CurrentCamera
		local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
		local ToolName = "Click Fling Ball"
		local IsToolEquipped = false
		local Backpack = LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack")
		if not Backpack:FindFirstChild(ToolName) then
			local ToolInstance = Instance.new("Tool")
			ToolInstance.Name = ToolName
			ToolInstance.RequiresHandle = false
			ToolInstance.CanBeDropped = false
			ToolInstance.Equipped:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu986
				IsToolEquipped = true
			end)
			ToolInstance.Unequipped:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu986
				IsToolEquipped = false
			end)
			ToolInstance.Parent = Backpack
		end
		local function HandlePlayer(TargetPlayer)
			local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
			local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
			local Character = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
			local CharacterRef = Character
			local Humanoid = Character.WaitForChild(CharacterRef, "Humanoid")
			local LocalPlayer = Character
			Character.WaitForChild(LocalPlayer, "HumanoidRootPart")
			local Backpack = LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack")
			local SoccerBallsFolder = workspace.WorkspaceCom:WaitForChild("001_SoccerBalls")
			local function FindSoccerBallFunction()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu996, (ref) vu992, (ref) vu997, (ref) vu991
				if not (Backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall") or Character:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall")) then
					game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "SoccerBall")
				end
				repeat
					task.wait()
				until Backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall") or Character:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall")
				local SoccerBallInstance = Backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall")
				if SoccerBallInstance then
					SoccerBallInstance.Parent = Character
				end
				repeat
					task.wait()
				until SoccerBallsFolder:FindFirstChild("Soccer" .. LocalPlayer.Name)
				return SoccerBallsFolder:FindFirstChild("Soccer" .. LocalPlayer.Name)
			end
			local Workspace = SoccerBallsFolder
			local SoccerBallClone = SoccerBallsFolder.FindFirstChild(Workspace, "Soccer" .. LocalPlayer.Name) or FindSoccerBallFunction()
			SoccerBallClone.CanCollide = false
			SoccerBallClone.Massless = true
			SoccerBallClone.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.new(0.0001, 0, 0)
			if TargetPlayer == LocalPlayer then
				-- ::l9::
				return
			else
				local PlayerCharacter = TargetPlayer.Character
				if not (PlayerCharacter and (PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("Humanoid"))) then
					-- goto l9
				end
				local HumanoidRootPart = PlayerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart
				local Humanoid = PlayerCharacter.Humanoid
				if SoccerBallClone:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BodyVelocity") then
					SoccerBallClone:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BodyVelocity"):Destroy()
				end
				local BodyVelocityInstance = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
				BodyVelocityInstance.Name = "FlingPower"
				BodyVelocityInstance.Velocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
				BodyVelocityInstance.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
				BodyVelocityInstance.MaxForce = math.huge
				BodyVelocityInstance.Parent = SoccerBallClone
				workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = Humanoid
				while true do
					if true then
						if HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude <= 0 then
							local ChildIterator, ChildTable, ChildIndex = pairs(PlayerCharacter:GetChildren())
							while true do
								local HitPart
								ChildIndex, HitPart = ChildIterator(ChildTable, ChildIndex)
								if ChildIndex == nil then
									break
								end
								if HitPart:IsA("BasePart") and (HitPart.CanCollide and not HitPart.Anchored) then
									SoccerBallClone.CFrame = HitPart.CFrame
									task.wait(0.00016666666666666666)
								end
							end
						else
							local PredictedPosition = HumanoidRootPart.Position + HumanoidRootPart.Velocity / 1.5
							SoccerBallClone.CFrame = CFrame.new(PredictedPosition)
							SoccerBallClone.Orientation = SoccerBallClone.Orientation + Vector3.new(45, 60, 30)
						end
					end
					task.wait(0.00016666666666666666)
					if HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude > 1000 or (Humanoid.Health <= 0 or (not PlayerCharacter:IsDescendantOf(workspace) or TargetPlayer.Parent ~= PlayersService)) then
						workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = Humanoid
						-- goto l9
					end
				end
			end
		end
		UserInputService.TouchTap:Connect(function(TouchPositions, IsGameProcessed)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu986, (ref) vu983, (ref) vu981, (ref) vu980, (ref) vu984, (ref) vu1011
			if IsToolEquipped and not IsGameProcessed then
				local FirstTouchPosition = TouchPositions[1]
				local ScreenRay = CurrentCamera:ScreenPointToRay(FirstTouchPosition.X, FirstTouchPosition.ScreenHeight)
				local RaycastResult = Workspace:Raycast(ScreenRay.Origin, ScreenRay.Direction * 1000)
				if RaycastResult and RaycastResult.Instance then
					local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:GetPlayerFromCharacter((RaycastResult.Instance:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")))
					if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer ~= LocalPlayer then
						HandlePlayer(TargetPlayer)
					end
				end
			end
		end)
	end

	["Callback"] = function()

		local IsFlingActive = false
		while true do

			CurrentTool, ToolInstance = NextToolPair(ToolList, CurrentTool)

				break

			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1018, (ref) vu1020, (ref) vu1019

				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1040, (ref) vu1036, (ref) vu1019, (ref) vu1041, (ref) vu1035
				if not (Backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall") or PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall")) then
					ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "SoccerBall")

					task.wait()
				until Backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall") or PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall")
				local FoundSoccerBall = Backpack:FindFirstChild("SoccerBall")

					FoundSoccerBall.Parent = PlayerCharacter

					SoccerBall:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BodyVelocity"):Destroy()

								if ChildIndex == nil then
									break
								end
								if CollidingPart:IsA("BasePart") and (CollidingPart.CanCollide and not CollidingPart.Anchored) then
									SoccerBall.CFrame = CollidingPart.CFrame
									task.wait(0.00016666666666666666)
								end
							end

							local PredictedPosition = HumanoidRootPart.Position + HumanoidRootPart.Velocity / 1.5
							SoccerBall.CFrame = CFrame.new(PredictedPosition)
							SoccerBall.Orientation = SoccerBall.Orientation + Vector3.new(45, 60, 30)

					end
					task.wait(0.00016666666666666666)
					if HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude > 1000 or (Humanoid.Health <= 0 or (not PlayerCharacter:IsDescendantOf(Workspace) or Player.Parent ~= Players)) then
						Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = Humanoid
						-- goto l9
					end
				end
			end
		end
		UserInputService.TouchTap:Connect(function(TouchInputs, IsGameProcessed)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1029, (ref) vu1022, (ref) vu1020, (ref) vu1018, (ref) vu1023, (ref) vu1055

					if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer ~= LocalPlayer then
						HandleEquipFunction(TargetPlayer)
					end
				end
			end
		end)

TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Click Kill Couch (Tool)",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local Players = game:GetService("Players")
		local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
		local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
		local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
		local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
		local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
		local CurrentCamera = Workspace.CurrentCamera
		local ToolName = "Click Kill Couch"
		local IsClickingCouch = false
		local SelectedCouchName = nil
		local HeartbeatConnection = nil
		local IsHoldingCouch = false
		local SofaInstance = nil
		local TargetCFrame = nil
		local TargetHumanoidRootPart = nil
		local PlayerBackpack = LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("Backpack")
		if not PlayerBackpack:FindFirstChild(ToolName) then
			local ToolInstance = Instance.new("Tool")
			ToolInstance.Name = ToolName
			ToolInstance.RequiresHandle = false
			ToolInstance.CanBeDropped = false
			ToolInstance.Equipped:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1070
				IsClickingCouch = true
			end)
			ToolInstance.Unequipped:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1070, (ref) vu1071
				IsClickingCouch = false
				SelectedCouchName = nil
				limparSofa()
			end)
			ToolInstance.Parent = PlayerBackpack
		end
		function limparSofa()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1072, (ref) vu1073, (ref) vu1067, (ref) vu1074, (ref) vu1075, (ref) vu1076
			if HeartbeatConnection then
				HeartbeatConnection:Disconnect()
				HeartbeatConnection = nil
			end
			if IsHoldingCouch then
				local PlayerCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
				local CouchInstance = PlayerCharacter and PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("Couch")
				if CouchInstance then
					CouchInstance.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
					IsHoldingCouch = false
				end
			end
			if SofaInstance then
				SofaInstance:Destroy()
				SofaInstance = nil
			end
			if getgenv().AntiSit then
				getgenv().AntiSit:Set(false)
			end
			local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
			if Character then
				Character = LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
			end
			if Character then
				Character:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics, true)
				Character:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp)
			end
			if TargetCFrame and TargetHumanoidRootPart then
				TargetHumanoidRootPart.CFrame = TargetCFrame
				TargetCFrame = nil
			end
		end
		function pegarSofa()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1067, (ref) vu1063, (ref) vu1073
			local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
			if Character then
				local Backpack = LocalPlayer.Backpack
				if not (Backpack:FindFirstChild("Couch") or Character:FindFirstChild("Couch")) then
					ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents["1Too1l"]:InvokeServer(unpack({ "PickingTools", "Couch" }))
					task.wait(0.1)
				end
				local CouchTool = Backpack:FindFirstChild("Couch") or Character:FindFirstChild("Couch")
				if CouchTool then
					CouchTool.Parent = Character
					IsHoldingCouch = true
				end
			end
		end
		function posAleatoriaAbaixo(CharacterInstance)
			local HumanoidRootPart = CharacterInstance:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			if not HumanoidRootPart then
				return Vector3.new()
			end
			local RandomOffset = Vector3.new(math.random(-2, 2), -5.1, math.random(-2, 2))
			return HumanoidRootPart.Position + RandomOffset
		end
		function tpAbaixo(TargetPlayer)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1067, (ref) vu1074, (ref) vu1065
			if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				local CharacterInstance = LocalPlayer.Character
				local HumanoidRootPart
				if CharacterInstance then
					HumanoidRootPart = CharacterInstance:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				else
					HumanoidRootPart = CharacterInstance
				end
				if CharacterInstance then
					CharacterInstance = CharacterInstance:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
				end
				if HumanoidRootPart and CharacterInstance then
					CharacterInstance:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics, false)
					if not SofaInstance then
						SofaInstance = Instance.new("Part")
						SofaInstance.Size = Vector3.new(10, 1, 10)
						SofaInstance.Anchored = true
						SofaInstance.CanCollide = true
						SofaInstance.Transparency = 0.5
						SofaInstance.Parent = Workspace
					end
					local TargetPosition = posAleatoriaAbaixo(TargetPlayer.Character)
					SofaInstance.Position = TargetPosition
					HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(TargetPosition)
					CharacterInstance:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics, true)
				end
			else
				return
			end
		end
		function arremessarComSofa(TargetPlayer)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1071, (ref) vu1067, (ref) vu1075, (ref) vu1076, (ref) vu1072, (ref) vu1064, (ref) vu1062
			if TargetPlayer then
				SelectedCouchName = TargetPlayer.Name
				local PlayerCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
				if PlayerCharacter then
					local HumanoidRootPart = PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					if HumanoidRootPart then
						HumanoidRootPart = PlayerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
					end
					TargetCFrame = HumanoidRootPart
					TargetHumanoidRootPart = PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					pegarSofa()
					HeartbeatConnection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu1062, (ref) vu1071
						local TargetPlayer = Players:FindFirstChild(SelectedCouchName)
						if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
							if getgenv().AntiSit then
								getgenv().AntiSit:Set(true)
							end
							tpAbaixo(TargetPlayer)
						else
							limparSofa()
						end
					end)
					task.spawn(function()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu1062, (ref) vu1071, (ref) vu1067, (ref) vu1075
						local TargetPlayer = Players:FindFirstChild(SelectedCouchName)
						while TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") do
							task.wait(0.05)
							if TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid.SeatPart then
								local TargetPosition = CFrame.new(265.46, -450.83, -59.93)
								TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = TargetPosition
								LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = TargetPosition
								task.wait(0.4)
								limparSofa()
								task.wait(0.2)
								if TargetCFrame then
									LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = TargetCFrame
								end
								break
							end
						end
					end)
				end
			else
				return
			end
		end
		UserInputService.TouchTap:Connect(function(TouchPositions, IsGameProcessed)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1070, (ref) vu1068, (ref) vu1065, (ref) vu1062, (ref) vu1067
			if IsClickingCouch and not IsGameProcessed then
				local MousePosition = TouchPositions[1]
				local ScreenRay = CurrentCamera:ScreenPointToRay(MousePosition.X, MousePosition.ScreenHeight)
				local RaycastResult = Workspace:Raycast(ScreenRay.Origin, ScreenRay.Direction * 1000)
				if RaycastResult and RaycastResult.Instance then
					local TargetPlayer = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter((RaycastResult.Instance:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")))
					if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer ~= LocalPlayer then
						arremessarComSofa(TargetPlayer)
					end
				end
			end
		end)
	end
})

	["Name"] = "All methods"
})
TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Kill All Bus",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
		local WorkspaceService = game:GetService("Workspace")
		local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
		local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
		local VoidPosition = Vector3.new(145.51, -374.09, 21.58)
		local SavedPlayerPosition = nil
		local function FindPlayerBus()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1105, (ref) vu1104
			local VehiclesFolder = WorkspaceService:FindFirstChild("Vehicles")
			if VehiclesFolder then
				return VehiclesFolder:FindFirstChild(PlayersService.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
			else
				return nil
			end
		end
		local function TrackPlayerAndExecuteCallback(PlayerName, CallbackFunction)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1104, (ref) vu1111, (ref) vu1108, (ref) vu1109, (ref) vu1107, (ref) vu1106
			while true do
				if PlayerName then
					local TargetPlayer = PlayersService:FindFirstChild(PlayerName)
					if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
						local TargetHumanoid = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
						if TargetHumanoid and TargetHumanoid.Sit then
							local SeatWeld = FindPlayerBus()
							if SeatWeld then
								SeatWeld:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(VoidPosition))
								print("Jogador sentou, levando \195\180nibus para o void!")
								task.wait(0.2)
								local function SimulateJump()
									-- upvalues: (ref) vu1104
									local Character = PlayersService.LocalPlayer.Character
									if Character then
										Character = PlayersService.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
									end
									if Character then
										Character:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping)
									end
								end
								SimulateJump()
								print("Simulando primeiro pulo!")
								task.wait(0.4)
								SimulateJump()
								print("Simulando segundo pulo!")
								task.wait(0.5)
								if SavedPlayerPosition then
									PlayersService.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = SavedPlayerPosition
									print("Player voltou para a posi\195\167\195\163o inicial Xique")
									task.wait(0.1)
									ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer(unpack({ "DeleteAllVehicles" }))
									print("Todos os ve\195\173culos foram deletados!")
								end
							end
							if CallbackFunction then
								CallbackFunction()
							end
							return
						end
						local HumanoidRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
						local TimeValue = tick() * 35
						local _ = math.sin(TimeValue) * 10
						local OffsetDistance = math.cos(TimeValue) * 20
						local TargetModel = FindPlayerBus()
						if TargetModel then
							TargetModel:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, OffsetDistance))
						end
					end
				end
				RunService.RenderStepped:Wait()
			end
		end
		local function ProcessPlayerRequest(PlayerName, CallbackFunction)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1104, (ref) vu1109, (ref) vu1111, (ref) vu1107, (ref) vu1123
			local TargetPlayerName = PlayerName
			local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
			local PlayerCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
			local HumanoidRootPart = PlayerCharacter:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			SavedPlayerPosition = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
			local TargetSeat = FindPlayerBus()
			if not TargetSeat then
				HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(1118.81, 75.998, -1138.61)
				task.wait(0.5)
				local RemoteEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("RE")
				if RemoteEvent and RemoteEvent:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r") then
					RemoteEvent["1Ca1r"]:FireServer("PickingCar", "SchoolBus")
				end
				task.wait(1)
				TargetSeat = FindPlayerBus()
			end
			if TargetSeat then
				local VehicleSeat = TargetSeat:FindFirstChild("Body")
				if VehicleSeat then
					VehicleSeat = TargetSeat.Body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
				end
				if VehicleSeat and (PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and not PlayerCharacter.Humanoid.Sit) then
					repeat
						HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 2, 0)
						task.wait()
					until PlayerCharacter.Humanoid.Sit or not TargetSeat.Parent
				end
			end
			spawn(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1123, (ref) vu1126, (ref) pu1125
				TrackPlayerAndExecuteCallback(TargetPlayerName, CallbackFunction)
			end)
		end
		local function ProcessPlayerQueue(PlayerQueue)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1133, (ref) vu1135
			if #PlayerQueue ~= 0 then
				ProcessPlayerRequest(table.remove(PlayerQueue, 1).Name, function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) vu1135, (ref) pu1134
					task.wait(0.5)
					ProcessPlayerQueue(PlayerQueue)
				end)
			end
		end
		local PlayersService = PlayersService
		ProcessPlayerQueue(PlayersService.GetPlayers(PlayersService))
	end
})

TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "House Ban kill All",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu4
		local ReplicatedStorageService = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
		local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
		local WorkspaceService = game:GetService("Workspace")
		local function ProcessPlayer(PlayerInstance)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1139, (ref) vu1137
			local LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
			local _ = LocalPlayer.Backpack
			local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
			local CharacterReference = Character
			local Humanoid = Character.FindFirstChildOfClass(CharacterReference, "Humanoid")
			local Character = Character
			local HumanoidRootPart = Character.FindFirstChild(Character, "HumanoidRootPart")
			local LotsFolder = game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("001_Lots")
			local _ = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
			local RotationAngle = 0
			local VehiclesFolder = WorkspaceService.Vehicles
			function Check()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1141, (ref) vu1142, (ref) vu1144, (ref) vu1146, (ref) vu1149
				return LocalPlayer and (Character and (Humanoid and (HumanoidRootPart and VehiclesFolder))) and true or false
			end
			if Check() then
				if not LotsFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "House") then
					local ChildIterator, ChildTable, ChildIndex = pairs(LotsFolder:GetChildren())
					local SelectedHouse = nil
					while true do
						local CurrentChild
						ChildIndex, CurrentChild = ChildIterator(ChildTable, ChildIndex)
						if ChildIndex == nil then
							break
						end
						if CurrentChild.Name == "For Sale" then
							local DescendantIterator, DescendantTable, DescendantIndex = pairs(CurrentChild:GetDescendants())
							while true do
								local NumberValue
								DescendantIndex, NumberValue = DescendantIterator(DescendantTable, DescendantIndex)
								if DescendantIndex == nil then
									break
								end
								if NumberValue:IsA("NumberValue") and (NumberValue.Name == "Number" and (NumberValue.Value < 25 and NumberValue.Value > 10)) then
									SelectedHouse = CurrentChild
									break
								end
							end
						end
					end
					local BuyHousePart = SelectedHouse:FindFirstChild("BuyHouse")
					local _ = BuyHousePart.Position
					if BuyHousePart and BuyHousePart:IsA("BasePart") then
						HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = BuyHousePart.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, -6, 0)
						task.wait(0.5)
						local ClickDetector = BuyHousePart:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector")
						if ClickDetector then
							fireclickdetector(ClickDetector)
						end
					end
				end
				task.wait(0.5)
				local PlayerHouse = LotsFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "House")
				if PlayerHouse then
					task.wait(0.5)
					local IteratorFunction, DescendantsTable, CurrentIndex = pairs(PlayerHouse:GetDescendants())
					local NumberValueInstance = nil
					while true do
						local CurrentDescendant
						CurrentIndex, CurrentDescendant = IteratorFunction(DescendantsTable, CurrentIndex)
						if CurrentIndex == nil then
							break
						end
						if CurrentDescendant.Name == "Number" then
							if CurrentDescendant:IsA("NumberValue") then
								NumberValueInstance = CurrentDescendant
							end
						end
					end
					task.wait(0.5)
					game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Gettin1gHous1e"):FireServer("PickingCustomHouse", "049_House", NumberValueInstance.Value)
				end
				task.wait(0.5)
				local Workspace = VehiclesFolder
				if not VehiclesFolder.FindFirstChild(Workspace, LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car") and Check() then
					HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(1118.81, 75.998, -1138.61)
					task.wait(0.5)
					game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer("PickingCar", "SchoolBus")
					task.wait(0.5)
					local Workspace = VehiclesFolder
					local PlayerCar = VehiclesFolder.FindFirstChild(Workspace, LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
					task.wait(0.5)
					local CarBody = PlayerCar:FindFirstChild("Body")
					if CarBody then
						CarBody = PlayerCar.Body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
					end
					if CarBody then
						repeat
							task.wait()
							HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CarBody.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, math.random(-1, 1), 0)
						until Humanoid.Sit
					end
				end
				task.wait(0.5)
				local Workspace = VehiclesFolder
				local VehicleInstance = VehiclesFolder.FindFirstChild(Workspace, LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
				if VehicleInstance then
					if not Humanoid.Sit then
						local VehicleBodyPart = VehicleInstance:FindFirstChild("Body")
						if VehicleBodyPart then
							VehicleBodyPart = VehicleInstance.Body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
						end
						if VehicleBodyPart then
							repeat
								task.wait()
								HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = VehicleBodyPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, math.random(-1, 1), 0)
							until Humanoid.Sit
						end
					end
					local PlayerCharacter = PlayerInstance.Character
					local Humanoid = PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
					local HumanoidRootPart = PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
					if PlayerCharacter and (Humanoid and (HumanoidRootPart and not Humanoid.Sit)) then
						while not Humanoid.Sit do
							task.wait()
							local function SetModelCFrame(PositionReference, OffsetCFrame, RotationCFrame)
								-- upvalues: (ref) vu1172
								VehicleInstance:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(PositionReference.Position) * OffsetCFrame * RotationCFrame)
							end
							RotationAngle = RotationAngle + 100
							SetModelCFrame(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
							SetModelCFrame(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
							SetModelCFrame(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(2.25, 1.5, -2.25) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
							SetModelCFrame(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(-2.25, -1.5, 2.25) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
							SetModelCFrame(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
							SetModelCFrame(HumanoidRootPart, CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0) + Humanoid.MoveDirection * HumanoidRootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.1, CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
						end
						task.wait(0.2)
						local PlayerHouse = LotsFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "House")
						VehicleInstance:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(PlayerHouse.HouseSpawnPosition.Position))
						task.wait(0.2)
						local PlayerRegion = Region3.new(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - Vector3.new(30, 30, 30), game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position + Vector3.new(30, 30, 30))
						local FoundParts = workspace:FindPartsInRegion3(PlayerRegion, game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart, math.huge)
						local IteratorFunction, CurrentIndex, CurrentValue = pairs(FoundParts)
						while true do
							local RootPart
							CurrentValue, RootPart = IteratorFunction(CurrentIndex, CurrentValue)
							if CurrentValue == nil then
								break
							end
							if RootPart.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then
								local BanArguments = { "BanPlayerFromHouse", game:GetService("Players"):FindFirstChild(RootPart.Parent.Name), RootPart.Parent }
								game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Playe1rTrigge1rEven1t"):FireServer(unpack(BanArguments))
							end
						end
					end
				end
			end
			ReplicatedStorageService:WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer(unpack({ "DeleteAllVehicles" }))
		end
		local PlayerIterator, PlayerList, PlayerIndex = pairs(PlayersService:GetPlayers())
		while true do
			local OtherPlayer
			PlayerIndex, OtherPlayer = PlayerIterator(PlayerList, PlayerIndex)
			if PlayerIndex == nil then
				break
			end
			if OtherPlayer ~= LocalPlayer then
				ProcessPlayer(OtherPlayer)
				task.wait(2)
			end
		end
	end
})

TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Fling Boat all",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
		local PlayerCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character
		local Humanoid = PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
		local HumanoidRootPart = PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local VehiclesFolder = game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Vehicles")
		local OriginalCFrame = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
		local RotationAngle = 0
		if not VehiclesFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car") and HumanoidRootPart then
			HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(1754, -2, 58)
			task.wait(0.5)
			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer("PickingBoat", "MilitaryBoatFree")
			task.wait(0.5)
			local PlayerCar = VehiclesFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
			task.wait(0.5)
			local CarBody = PlayerCar:FindFirstChild("Body")
			if CarBody then
				CarBody = PlayerCar.Body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
			end
			if CarBody then
				repeat
					task.wait()
					HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CarBody.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, math.random(-1, 1), 0)
				until Humanoid.Sit
			end
		end
		task.wait(0.5)
		local PlayerCarInstance = VehiclesFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
		if PlayerCarInstance and not Humanoid.Sit then
			local CarBodyPart = PlayerCarInstance:FindFirstChild("Body")
			if CarBodyPart then
				CarBodyPart = PlayerCarInstance.Body:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")
			end
			if CarBodyPart then
				repeat
					task.wait()
					HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CarBodyPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, math.random(-1, 1), 0)
				until Humanoid.Sit
			end
		end
		local BodyGyro = Instance.new("BodyGyro")
		BodyGyro.Parent = PlayerCarInstance.PrimaryPart
		BodyGyro.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(10000000, 10000000, 10000000)
		BodyGyro.MaxForce = 10000000
		BodyGyro.CFrame = PlayerCarInstance.PrimaryPart.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(90), 0)
		local function HandleCharacterAnimation(_, Character, _)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1200, (ref) vu1203
			RotationAngle = 0
			local AnimationEndTime = tick() + 1
			while tick() < AnimationEndTime do
				RotationAngle = RotationAngle + 100
				task.wait()
				local function SetModelCFrame(PositionReference, OffsetCFrame, RotationCFrame)
					-- upvalues: (ref) vu1203
					PlayerCarInstance:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(PositionReference.Position) * OffsetCFrame * RotationCFrame)
				end
				SetModelCFrame(Character, CFrame.new(0, 3, 0), CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
				SetModelCFrame(Character, CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 2), CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
				SetModelCFrame(Character, CFrame.new(2, 1.5, 2.25), CFrame.Angles(math.rad(50), 0, 0))
				SetModelCFrame(Character, CFrame.new(-2.25, -1.5, 2.25), CFrame.Angles(math.rad(30), 0, 0))
				SetModelCFrame(Character, CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0), CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
				SetModelCFrame(Character, CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0), CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0))
			end
		end
		local PlayerIterator, PlayerListState, PlayerIterator = pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())
		while true do
			local OtherPlayer
			PlayerIterator, OtherPlayer = PlayerIterator(PlayerListState, PlayerIterator)
			if PlayerIterator == nil then
				break
			end
			if OtherPlayer ~= LocalPlayer then
				local OtherCharacter = OtherPlayer.Character
				local OtherHumanoid
				if OtherCharacter then
					OtherHumanoid = OtherCharacter:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
				else
					OtherHumanoid = OtherCharacter
				end
				local HumanoidRootPart
				if OtherCharacter then
					HumanoidRootPart = OtherCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				else
					HumanoidRootPart = OtherCharacter
				end
				if OtherCharacter and (OtherHumanoid and HumanoidRootPart) then
					HandleCharacterAnimation(OtherCharacter, HumanoidRootPart, OtherHumanoid)
				end
			end
		end
		task.wait(0.5)
		PlayerCarInstance:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.new(0, 0, 0))
		task.wait(0.5)
		Humanoid.Sit = false
		task.wait(0.5)
		HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = OriginalCFrame
		BodyGyro:Destroy()
	end
})
