TrollTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Auto Fling All",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
		local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
		local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
		local CurrentCamera = workspace.CurrentCamera
		local function SpectatePlayer(TargetPlayer)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1222, (ref) vu1221, (ref) vu1223
			if TargetPlayer and (TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer ~= LocalPlayer) then
				local IsSpectating = true
				local CharacterRootPart = LocalPlayer.Character
				if CharacterRootPart then
					CharacterRootPart = LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				end
				local CharacterRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character
				if CharacterRootPart then
					CharacterRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				end
				if CharacterRootPart and CharacterRootPart then
					local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
					local Humanoid = Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
					local OriginalCFrame = CharacterRootPart.CFrame
					ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Clea1rTool1s"):FireServer("ClearAllTools")
					task.wait(0.2)
					ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "Couch")
					task.wait(0.3)
					local CouchTool = LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Couch")
					if CouchTool then
						CouchTool.Parent = Character
					end
					task.wait(0.1)
					game:GetService("VirtualInputManager"):SendKeyEvent(true, Enum.KeyCode.FKey, false, game)
					task.wait(0.25)
					workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = 0 / 0
					local FlingVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
					FlingVelocity.Name = "FlingForce"
					FlingVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
					FlingVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
					FlingVelocity.Parent = CharacterRootPart
					Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, false)
					Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
					CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") or (CharacterRootPart or Humanoid)
					task.spawn(function()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu1226, (ref) vu1225, (ref) pu1224, (ref) vu1232, (ref) vu1229, (ref) vu1230, (ref) vu1223, (ref) vu1228, (ref) vu1221
						local ParticleList = { CharacterRootPart }
						local RotationAngle = 0
						while IsSpectating and (TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character) and (TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") and not TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid").Sit) do
							RotationAngle = RotationAngle + 50
							local IteratorFunction, ParticleTable, ParticleIndex = ipairs(ParticleList)
							while true do
								local IteratorIndex
								ParticleIndex, IteratorIndex = IteratorFunction(ParticleTable, ParticleIndex)
								if ParticleIndex == nil then
									break
								end
								local HumanoidRootPart = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
								local PredictedPosition = HumanoidRootPart.Position + HumanoidRootPart.Velocity / 1.5
								CharacterRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(PredictedPosition) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(RotationAngle), 0, 0)
							end
							CharacterRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
							CharacterRootPart.RotVelocity = Vector3.new(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
							task.wait()
						end
						IsSpectating = false
						FlingVelocity:Destroy()
						Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true)
						Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
						CharacterRootPart.CFrame = OriginalCFrame
						CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = Humanoid
						local CharacterModel = Character
						local DescendantsIterator, DescendantsTable, CurrentDescendant = pairs(CharacterModel:GetDescendants())
						while true do
							local DescendantInstance
							CurrentDescendant, DescendantInstance = DescendantsIterator(DescendantsTable, CurrentDescendant)
							if CurrentDescendant == nil then
								break
							end
							if DescendantInstance:IsA("BasePart") then
								DescendantInstance.Velocity = Vector3.zero
								DescendantInstance.RotVelocity = Vector3.zero
							end
						end
						Humanoid:UnequipTools()
						ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l"):InvokeServer("PickingTools", "Couch")
					end)
					while IsSpectating do
						task.wait()
					end
				end
			else
				return
			end
		end
		local PlayerIterator, PlayerList, CurrentPlayer = ipairs(PlayersService:GetPlayers())
		while true do
			local CurrentTool
			CurrentPlayer, CurrentTool = PlayerIterator(PlayerList, CurrentPlayer)
			if CurrentPlayer == nil then
				break
			end
			SpectatePlayer(CurrentTool)
		end
	end
})

end

local RGBColors = {
	Color3.new(1, 0, 0),
	Color3.new(0, 1, 0),
	Color3.new(0, 0, 1),
	Color3.new(1, 1, 0),
	Color3.new(0, 1, 1),
	Color3.new(1, 0, 1)
}
local IsRGBEnabled = false
local function RGBEffectLoop()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1417, (ref) vu1416
	local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
	local RemoteEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("RE")
	if RemoteEvent then
		RemoteEvent = ReplicatedStorage.ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Player1sHous1e")
	end
	if RemoteEvent then
		while IsRGBEnabled do
			local IteratorFunction, TableToIterate, CurrentIndex = ipairs(RGBColors)
			while true do
				local HouseInstance
				CurrentIndex, HouseInstance = IteratorFunction(TableToIterate, CurrentIndex)
				if CurrentIndex == nil then
					break
				end
				if not IsRGBEnabled then
					return
				end
				local EventArguments = { "ColorPickHouse", HouseInstance }
				pcall(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) vu1419, (ref) vu1424
					RemoteEvent:FireServer(unpack(EventArguments))
				end)
				task.wait(0.8)
			end
		end
	else
		warn("RemoteEvent \'1Player1sHous1e\' n\195\163o encontrado.")
	end
end
local function UnbanPlayerFunction(PlayerToUnban)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1417, (ref) vu1425
	IsRGBEnabled = PlayerToUnban
	if IsRGBEnabled then
		print("House RGB Activated")
		spawn(RGBEffectLoop)
	else
		print("House RGB Deactivated")
	end
end

local SelectedHouseName = nil
local DoorToggle = nil
local function GetHouseList()
	local HouseNames = {}
	local LotModels = workspace:FindFirstChild("001_Lots")
	if LotModels then
		local IteratorFunction, ChildIndex, ChildInstance = ipairs(LotModels:GetChildren())
		while true do
			local CurrentChild
			ChildInstance, CurrentChild = IteratorFunction(ChildIndex, ChildInstance)
			if ChildInstance == nil then
				break
			end
			if CurrentChild.Name ~= "For Sale" and CurrentChild:IsA("Model") then
				table.insert(HouseNames, CurrentChild.Name)
			end
		end
	end
	return HouseNames
end

		HousesTab:AddDropdown({
			["Name"] = "Selecione a Casa",
			["Options"] = HouseList,
			["Default"] = "...",
			["Callback"] = function(SelectedHouseOption)
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1430, (ref) vu1431
				SelectedHouseName = SelectedHouseOption
				if DoorToggle then
					DoorToggle:Set(false)
				end
			end
		})
	end)
end

				local SafePart = LotInstance.HousePickedByPlayer.HouseModel:FindFirstChild("001_Safe")

					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(SafePart.WorldPivot.Position)

				end

				print("Casa n\195\163o encontrada: " .. tostring(SelectedHouseName))
			end
		end
	})

pcall(function()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1431, (ref) vu1429, (ref) vu1430
	DoorToggle = HousesTab:AddToggle({
		["Name"] = "Atravessar Porta da Casa",
		["Description"] = "",
		["Default"] = false,
		["Callback"] = function(IsCollisionEnabled)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1430
			pcall(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1430, (ref) pu1446
				local LotInstanceForCollision = workspace["001_Lots"]:FindFirstChild(tostring(SelectedHouseName))
				if LotInstanceForCollision and LotInstanceForCollision:FindFirstChild("HousePickedByPlayer") then
					local HouseDoorsInstance = LotInstanceForCollision.HousePickedByPlayer.HouseModel:FindFirstChild("001_HouseDoors")
					if HouseDoorsInstance and HouseDoorsInstance:FindFirstChild("HouseDoorFront") then
						local IteratorFunction, ChildInstance, IteratorState = ipairs(HouseDoorsInstance.HouseDoorFront:GetChildren())
						while true do
							local TargetPart
							IteratorState, TargetPart = IteratorFunction(ChildInstance, IteratorState)
							if IteratorState == nil then
								break
							end
							if TargetPart:IsA("BasePart") then
								TargetPart.CanCollide = not IsCollisionEnabled
							end
						end
					end
				end
			end)
		end
	})
end)

	local NextValue
	TableValue, NextValue = IteratorFunction(TableKey, TableValue)
	if TableValue == nil then
		break
	end
	table.insert(HouseOptions, TableValue)
end

	return (tonumber(FirstString:match("%d+")) or 0) < (tonumber(SecondString:match("%d+")) or 0)
end)

function startAutoUnban()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1428
	while IsAutoUnbanActive do
		pcall(function()
			local IteratorFunction, DescendantsTable, CurrentKey = pairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):WaitForChild("001_Lots"):GetDescendants())
			while true do
				local CurrentInstance
				CurrentKey, CurrentInstance = IteratorFunction(DescendantsTable, CurrentKey)
				if CurrentKey == nil then
					break
				end
				if CurrentInstance.Name:match("^BannedBlock%d+$") then
					CurrentInstance:Destroy()
				end
			end
		end)
		task.wait(1)
	end
end

local CurrentAudioId = nil
AudioTab:AddTextBox({
	["Name"] = "Insira o ID do \195\129udio ou Musica",
	["Description"] = "Digite o ID do \195\161udio",
	["PlaceholderText"] = "ID do \195\161udio",
	["Callback"] = function(InputAudioId)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1478
		CurrentAudioId = tonumber(InputAudioId)
	end
})
local IndexIterator, AudioIdsTable, AudioEntry = ipairs(AudioIds)
local SelectedAudioId = CurrentAudioId
local AudioNameList = {}
while true do
	local AudioObject
	AudioEntry, AudioObject = IndexIterator(AudioIdsTable, AudioEntry)
	if AudioEntry == nil then
		break
	end
	table.insert(AudioNameList, AudioObject.Name)
end
AudioTab:AddDropdown({
	["Name"] = "Selecione o \195\129udio",
	["Description"] = "Escolha um \195\161udio da lista",
	["Options"] = AudioNameList,
	["Default"] = AudioNameList[1],
	["Flag"] = "selected_audio",
	["Callback"] = function(SelectedAudioName)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1477, (ref) vu1483
		local IteratorFunction, TableToIterate, CurrentIndex = ipairs(AudioIds)
		while true do
			local CurrentValue
			CurrentIndex, CurrentValue = IteratorFunction(TableToIterate, CurrentIndex)
			if CurrentIndex == nil then
				break
			end
			if CurrentValue.Name == SelectedAudioName then
				SelectedAudioId = CurrentValue.ID
				break
			end
		end
	end
})
local IsAudioLoopEnabled = false
AudioTab:AddSection({ "Loop de Audio" })
local function AudioLoopFunction()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1491, (ref) vu1483
	while IsAudioLoopEnabled do
		if SelectedAudioId then
			local SoundArguments = { game:GetService("Workspace"), SelectedAudioId, 1 }
			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Gu1nSound1s"):FireServer(unpack(SoundArguments))
			local SoundInstance = Instance.new("Sound")
			SoundInstance.SoundId = "rbxassetid://" .. SelectedAudioId
			SoundInstance.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
			SoundInstance:Play()
		else
			warn("Nenhum \195\161udio selecionado!")
		end
		task.wait(0.5)
	end
end
AudioTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Loop Tocar \195\129udio",
	["Description"] = "Ativa o loop do \195\161udio",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Flag"] = "audio_loop",
	["Callback"] = function(LoopEnabled)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1491, (ref) vu1494
		IsAudioLoopEnabled = LoopEnabled
		if IsAudioLoopEnabled then
			task.spawn(AudioLoopFunction)
		end
	end
})
AudioTab:AddParagraph({ "Info", "Loop de tocar \195\129udio (Todos players do Server ouvem)" })
local function PlayAudioLoop()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1483
	if SelectedAudioId then
		local LoopSoundArguments = { game:GetService("Workspace"), SelectedAudioId, 1 }
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Gu1nSound1s"):FireServer(unpack(LoopSoundArguments))
		local SoundEffect = Instance.new("Sound")
		SoundEffect.SoundId = "rbxassetid://" .. SelectedAudioId
		SoundEffect.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart
		SoundEffect:Play()
	else
		warn("Nenhum \195\161udio selecionado!")
	end
end
AudioTab:AddSection({ "Tocar \195\129udio" })
AudioTab:AddButton({ "Tocar \195\129udio", function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1498
		PlayAudioLoop()
	end })
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local SoundAssetId = 6314880174
local function PlaySoundEffect(SoundId)
	local function FindAudioContainer()
		local AudioFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Audio all client")
		if not AudioFolder then
			AudioFolder = Instance.new("Folder")
			AudioFolder.Name = "Audio all client"
			AudioFolder.Parent = workspace
		end
		return AudioFolder
	end;
	(function(SoundId)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1503
		if type(SoundId) ~= "number" then
			print("Insira um n\195\186mero v\195\161lido!")
			return nil
		end
		local AudioFolderInstance = FindAudioContainer()
		if AudioFolderInstance then
			local SoundInstance = Instance.new("Sound")
			SoundInstance.SoundId = "rbxassetid://" .. SoundId
			SoundInstance.Volume = 1
			SoundInstance.Looped = false
			SoundInstance.Parent = AudioFolderInstance
			SoundInstance:Play()
			task.wait(1)
			SoundInstance:Destroy()
		end
	end)(SoundId)
end
local function PlaySound(SoundId)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1499
	if type(SoundId) ~= "number" then
		print("Insira um n\195\186mero v\195\161lido!")
		return nil
	end
	local SoundRemoteEvent = ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("1Gu1nSound1s", true)
	if SoundRemoteEvent then
		SoundRemoteEvent:FireServer(workspace, SoundId, 1)
	end
end
AudioTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Estorar ouvido de geral KK",
	["Description"] = "Toca \195\161udio repetidamente para todos",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Flag"] = "audio_spam",
	["Callback"] = function(IsToggled)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1510, (ref) vu1500, (ref) vu1507
		getgenv().Audio_All_loop_fast = IsToggled
		while getgenv().Audio_All_loop_fast do
			PlaySound(SoundAssetId)
			task.spawn(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1507, (ref) vu1500
				PlaySoundEffect(SoundAssetId)
			end)
			task.wait(0.03)
		end
	end
})

local LagServerTab = MainWindow:MakeTab({ "Lag Server", "bomb" })
LagServerTab:AddSection({
	["Name"] = "Lags Experimentais"
})
local IsLagLoopActive = false
local LagLoopCoroutine = nil
LagServerTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Lag com \195\148nibus",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(IsToggled)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1513, (ref) vu1514
		IsLagLoopActive = IsToggled
		if IsLagLoopActive then
			local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
			local ReplicatedStorageService = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
			local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
			if not LocalPlayer then
				warn("LocalPlayer n\195\163o encontrado.")
				return
			end
			local HumanoidRootPart = (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()):WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart", 5)
			if not HumanoidRootPart then
				warn("HumanoidRootPart n\195\163o encontrado.")
				return
			end
			local function TeleportAndPickCar()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1518
				local VehiclesFolder = workspace:FindFirstChild("Vehicles")
				if VehiclesFolder then
					return VehiclesFolder:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
				else
					return nil
				end
			end
			local RemoteEventContainer = ReplicatedStorageService:FindFirstChild("RE")
			if not RemoteEventContainer then
				warn("RemoteEvent \'RE\' n\195\163o encontrado em ReplicatedStorage.")
				return
			end
			if not RemoteEventContainer:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r") then
				warn("Evento filho \'1Ca1r\' n\195\163o encontrado dentro de \'RE\'.")
				return
			end
			LagLoopCoroutine = coroutine.wrap(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1513, (ref) vu1519, (ref) vu1521, (ref) vu1522
				while IsLagLoopActive do
					local Success, Error = pcall(function()
						-- upvalues: (ref) vu1519, (ref) vu1521, (ref) vu1522
						HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(1118.81, 75.998, -1138.61)
						TeleportAndPickCar()
						RemoteEventContainer["1Ca1r"]:FireServer("PickingCar", "SchoolBus")
					end)
					if not Success then
						warn("Erro ao executar lag loop: " .. tostring(Error))
						IsLagLoopActive = false
						break
					end
					task.wait(0)
				end
			end)
			LagLoopCoroutine()
		end
	end
})
LagServerTab:AddSection({
	["Name"] = "Lag com Laptop"
})
local LagSettings = {
	["LagLaptop"] = false
}
local function InteractWithPart(TargetPart)
	local ClickDetector = TargetPart:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("ClickDetector")
	if ClickDetector then
		fireclickdetector(ClickDetector)
	end
end
local function TeleportAndClickLoop(TargetCFrame, IterationCount)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1525, (ref) vu1528
	if TargetCFrame then
		local CurrentIteration = 0
		while CurrentIteration < IterationCount and LagSettings.LagLaptop do
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = TargetCFrame.CFrame
			InteractWithPart(TargetCFrame)
			CurrentIteration = CurrentIteration + 1
			wait(0.0001)
		end
	else
		warn("Laptop n\195\163o encontrado.")
	end
end

local CarTab = MainWindow:MakeTab({ "Carro", "car" })
local CarColors = {
	Color3.new(1, 0, 0),
	Color3.new(0, 1, 0),
	Color3.new(0, 0, 1),
	Color3.new(1, 1, 0),
	Color3.new(1, 0, 1),
	Color3.new(0, 1, 1),
	Color3.new(0.5, 0, 0.5),
	Color3.new(1, 0.5, 0)
}
local CarRemoteEvent = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Player1sCa1r")
local IsRunning = false
local CoroutineHandle = nil
local function MainLoop()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1565, (ref) vu1563, (ref) vu1564
	while IsRunning do
		local IteratorFunction, TableValue, Index = ipairs(CarColors)
		while true do
			local SelectedColor3
			Index, SelectedColor3 = IteratorFunction(TableValue, Index)
			if Index == nil then
				break
			end
			if not IsRunning then
				return
			end
			CarRemoteEvent:FireServer(unpack({ "PickingCarColor", SelectedColor3 }))
			wait(1)
		end
	end
end
CarTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Remove All Cars",
	["Callback"] = function()
		if false ~= true then
			local OriginalCFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(1754, -2, 58)
			wait(0.3)
			game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer(unpack({ "PickingBoat", "MilitaryBoatFree" }))
			wait(1)
			local VehicleDescendantsIterator, VehicleDescendantsState, VehicleDescendant = pairs(game.workspace.Vehicles[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car"]:GetDescendants())
			local VehicleSeat = nil
			while true do
				local VehicleSeatOrIteratorValue
				VehicleDescendant, VehicleSeatOrIteratorValue = VehicleDescendantsIterator(VehicleDescendantsState, VehicleDescendant)
				if VehicleDescendant == nil then
					break
				end
				if VehicleSeatOrIteratorValue:IsA("VehicleSeat") then
					VehicleSeat = VehicleSeatOrIteratorValue
				end
			end
			while game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health ~= 0 do
				if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit == true and not game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.SeatPart == VehicleSeat then
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
				end
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = VehicleSeat.CFrame
				task.wait()
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = VehicleSeat.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
				task.wait()
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = VehicleSeat.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, -1, 0)
				task.wait()
				if game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.SeatPart == VehicleSeat then
					local VehiclePartsIterator, VehiclePartsTable, VehicleIterator = pairs(game.workspace.Vehicles[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car"]:GetDescendants())
					while true do
						local VehiclePart
						VehicleIterator, VehiclePart = VehiclePartsIterator(VehiclePartsTable, VehicleIterator)
						if VehicleIterator == nil then
							break
						end
						if VehiclePart.Name == "PhysicalWheel" then
							VehiclePart:Destroy()
						end
					end
					local FlingThrust = Instance.new("BodyThrust", game.workspace.Vehicles[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car"].Chassis.Mass)
					FlingThrust.Force = Vector3.new(50000, 0, 50000)
					FlingThrust.Name = "SUNTERIUM HUB FLING"
					FlingThrust.Location = game.workspace.Vehicles[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car"].Chassis.Mass.Position
					local VehicleIterator2, CurrentKey, CurrentValue = pairs(game.workspace.Vehicles:GetChildren())
					while true do
						local Descendants
						CurrentValue, Descendants = VehicleIterator2(CurrentKey, CurrentValue)
						if CurrentValue == nil then
							break
						end
						local DescendantIterator, DescendantTable, Descendant = pairs(Descendants:GetDescendants())
						while true do
							local PhysicsPart
							Descendant, PhysicsPart = DescendantIterator(DescendantTable, Descendant)
							if Descendant == nil then
								break
							end
							if PhysicsPart.Name == "VehicleSeat" then
								local BodyVelocityInstance = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", game.workspace.Vehicles[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car"].Chassis.Mass)
								BodyVelocityInstance.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
								BodyVelocityInstance.MaxForce = 1250
								BodyVelocityInstance.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
								BodyVelocityInstance.Name = "#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W"
								for _ = 1, 25 do
									local Accumulator = {
										["x"] = 0,
										["y"] = 0,
										["z"] = 0,
										["x"] = PhysicsPart.Position.X,
										["y"] = PhysicsPart.Position.ScreenHeight,
										["z"] = PhysicsPart.Position.Position
									}
									Accumulator.PositionX = Accumulator.PositionX + PhysicsPart.Velocity.X / 2
									Accumulator.YCoordinate = Accumulator.YCoordinate + PhysicsPart.Velocity.ScreenHeight / 2
									Accumulator.z = Accumulator.z + PhysicsPart.Velocity.Position / 2
									if Accumulator.YCoordinate > -200 then
										game.workspace.Vehicles[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car"].Chassis.Mass.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(Accumulator.PositionX, Accumulator.YCoordinate, Accumulator.z))
										task.wait()
										game.workspace.Vehicles[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car"].Chassis.Mass.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(Accumulator.PositionX, Accumulator.YCoordinate, Accumulator.z)) + Vector3.new(0, -2, 0)
										task.wait()
										game.workspace.Vehicles[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car"].Chassis.Mass.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(Accumulator.PositionX, Accumulator.YCoordinate, Accumulator.z)) * CFrame.new(0, 0, 2)
										task.wait()
										game.workspace.Vehicles[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car"].Chassis.Mass.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(Accumulator.PositionX, Accumulator.YCoordinate, Accumulator.z)) * CFrame.new(2, 0, 0)
										task.wait()
									else
										game.workspace.Vehicles[game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car"].Chassis.Mass.CFrame = CFrame.new(0, 1000, 0)
									end
									task.wait()
								end
							end
						end
					end
					task.wait()
					game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer(unpack({ "DeleteAllVehicles" }))
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
					wait()
					local BodyVelocityInstance = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart)
					BodyVelocityInstance.MaxForce = Vector3.new(math.huge, math.huge, math.huge)
					BodyVelocityInstance.MaxForce = 1250
					BodyVelocityInstance.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
					BodyVelocityInstance.Name = "#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W"
					wait(0.1)
					for _ = 1, 2 do
						task.wait()
						game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = OriginalCFrame
					end
					wait(1)
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = OriginalCFrame
					wait()
					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("#mOVOOEPF$#@F$#GERE..>V<<<<EW<V<<W"):Destroy()
					wait(0.2)
					return
				end
			end
		end
	end
})

local SpeedValue = 50
local OtherValue = 50
local function UpdatePlayerValues(TopSpeedValue, TurboValue)
	local LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	local PlayerVehicle = workspace.Vehicles:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name .. "Car")
	if PlayerVehicle then
		local VehicleSeat = PlayerVehicle:FindFirstChild("Body").VehicleSeat
		if VehicleSeat then
			VehicleSeat.TopSpeed.Value = TopSpeedValue
			VehicleSeat.Turbo.Value = TurboValue
			wait(0.1)
			redzlib:MakeNotification({
				["Name"] = "Original by Kit Kat Hub",
				["Content"] = "Done, You can Move Now!",
				["Time"] = 5
			})
		else
			redzlib:MakeNotification({
				["Name"] = "Error",
				["Content"] = "Sit in car first!",
				["Time"] = 5
			})
		end
	else
		redzlib:MakeNotification({
			["Name"] = "Error",
			["Content"] = "Put a Car First!",
			["Time"] = 5
		})
	end
end

CarTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Turbo V2 [Melhor]",
	["Callback"] = function()
		local LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
		local HumanoidRootPart = (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()):FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local IsSpeedActive = false
		local MoveVelocity = 30
		local ControlGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui", LocalPlayer.PlayerGui)
		local function CreateControlButton(_, ButtonPosition, ImageId, Rotation, ClickCallback)
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1615
			local ImageButton = Instance.new("ImageButton", ControlGui)
			ImageButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 60, 0, 60)
			ImageButton.Position = ButtonPosition
			ImageButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
			ImageButton.Image = "rbxassetid://" .. ImageId
			ImageButton.Rotation = Rotation
			ImageButton.MouseButton1Down:Connect(ClickCallback)
			return ImageButton
		end
		local ForwardButton = CreateControlButton("BotaoFrente", UDim2.new(0, 10, 0.35, 0), "18478249606", 0, function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1613, (ref) vu1612, (ref) vu1614
			IsSpeedActive = true
			while IsSpeedActive do
				if HumanoidRootPart then
					HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * MoveVelocity
				end
				task.wait()
			end
		end)
		local BackButton = CreateControlButton("BotaoTras", UDim2.new(0, 10, 0.5, 0), "18478249606", 180, function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1613, (ref) vu1612, (ref) vu1614
			IsSpeedActive = true
			while IsSpeedActive do
				if HumanoidRootPart then
					HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = -HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * MoveVelocity
				end
				task.wait()
			end
		end)
		local LeftButton = CreateControlButton("BotaoEsquerda", UDim2.new(1, -210, 0.3, 0), "18478249606", -90, function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1613, (ref) vu1612, (ref) vu1614
			IsSpeedActive = true
			while IsSpeedActive do
				if HumanoidRootPart then
					HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = -HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.RightVector * MoveVelocity
				end
				task.wait()
			end
		end)
		local RightButton = CreateControlButton("BotaoDireita", UDim2.new(1, -140, 0.3, 0), "18478249606", 90, function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1613, (ref) vu1612, (ref) vu1614
			IsSpeedActive = true
			while IsSpeedActive do
				if HumanoidRootPart then
					HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.RightVector * MoveVelocity
				end
				task.wait()
			end
		end)
		local function HandleButtonRelease()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1613, (ref) vu1612
			IsSpeedActive = false
			if HumanoidRootPart then
				HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
			end
		end
		ForwardButton.MouseButton1Up:Connect(HandleButtonRelease)
		BackButton.MouseButton1Up:Connect(HandleButtonRelease)
		LeftButton.MouseButton1Up:Connect(HandleButtonRelease)
		RightButton.MouseButton1Up:Connect(HandleButtonRelease)
		local CloseButton = Instance.new("ImageButton", ControlGui)
		CloseButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 60, 0, 60)
		CloseButton.Position = UDim2.new(1, -130, 0, 10)
		CloseButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		CloseButton.Image = "rbxassetid://97607579386418"
		CloseButton.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1614
			MoveVelocity = 300
		end)
		local ToggleButton = Instance.new("TextButton", ControlGui)
		ToggleButton.Size = UDim2.new(0, 60, 0, 60)
		ToggleButton.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10)
		ToggleButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		ToggleButton.Text = "-"
		ToggleButton.TextSize = 40
		ToggleButton.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
		local ToggleStates = {
			ForwardButton,
			BackButton,
			LeftButton,
			RightButton,
			CloseButton
		}
		local IsToggled = false
		local function ToggleVisibility()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1630, (ref) vu1629, (ref) vu1628
			IsToggled = not IsToggled
			local IteratorIndex, CurrentValue, IteratorState = ipairs(ToggleStates)
			while true do
				local ChildInstance
				IteratorState, ChildInstance = IteratorIndex(CurrentValue, IteratorState)
				if IteratorState == nil then
					break
				end
				ChildInstance.Visible = not IsToggled
			end
			if IsToggled then
				ToggleButton.Text = "+"
			else
				ToggleButton.Text = "-"
			end
		end
		ToggleButton.MouseButton1Down:Connect(ToggleVisibility)
	end
})

local function SetCarMusicText(CarMusicText)
	if CarMusicText and CarMusicText ~= "" then
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Player1sCa1r"):FireServer(unpack({ "PickingCarMusicText", CarMusicText }))
	end
end
local function SetVehicleMotorState(VehicleModelName)
	if VehicleModelName and VehicleModelName ~= "" then
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1NoMoto1rVehicle1s"):FireServer(unpack({ "PickingScooterMusicText", VehicleModelName }))
	end
end
local function SetVehiclePickState(MusicId)
	if MusicId and MusicId ~= "" then
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Player1sHous1e"):FireServer(unpack({ "PickHouseMusicText", MusicId }))
	end
end
CarTab:AddTextBox({
	["Name"] = "Music ID (Gamepass Required)",
	["PlaceholderText"] = "Enter Music ID",
	["Callback"] = function(MusicIdInput)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1637, (ref) vu1639, (ref) vu1641
		SetCarMusicText(MusicIdInput)
		SetVehicleMotorState(MusicIdInput)
		SetVehiclePickState(MusicIdInput)
	end
})

CarTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Car RGB",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(ToggleState)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1565, (ref) vu1566, (ref) vu1571
		IsRunning = ToggleState
		if IsRunning then
			CoroutineHandle = coroutine.create(MainLoop)
			coroutine.resume(CoroutineHandle)
		end
	end
})

local IsHornSpamming = false
local HornArguments = { "Horn" }
local function HornSpamLoop()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1645, (ref) vu1564, (ref) vu1646
	while IsHornSpamming do
		CarRemoteEvent:FireServer(unpack(HornArguments))
		wait(0.1)
	end
end
CarTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Spam Horn",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(ShouldSpamHorns)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1645, (ref) vu1647
		IsHornSpamming = ShouldSpamHorns
		if IsHornSpamming then
			spawn(HornSpamLoop)
		end
	end
})

local IsSpammingVehicles = false
local function SpawnVehicle(VehicleName)
	game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("RE"):WaitForChild("1Ca1r"):FireServer(unpack({ "PickingCar", VehicleName }))
end
CarTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Spam Cars",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(IsEnabled)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1674, (ref) vu1673, (ref) vu1676
		IsSpammingVehicles = IsEnabled
		if IsSpammingVehicles then
			task.spawn(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1674, (ref) vu1673, (ref) vu1676
				while IsSpammingVehicles do
					local Iterator, Element, Index = ipairs(VehicleNames)
					while true do
						local Item
						Index, Item = Iterator(Element, Index)
						if Index == nil or not IsSpammingVehicles then
							break
						end
						SpawnVehicle(Item)
						wait(0.4)
					end
				end
			end)
		end
	end
})
CarTab:AddParagraph({ "Informa\195\167\195\163o:", "Spamar v\195\161rios carros" })
local LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local PlayerList = {}
local function MainLoop()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1683
	PlayerList = {}
	local PlayerIterator, PlayerList, PlayerIndex = pairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())
	while true do
		local CurrentPlayer
		PlayerIndex, CurrentPlayer = PlayerIterator(PlayerList, PlayerIndex)
		if PlayerIndex == nil then
			break
		end
		table.insert(PlayerList, CurrentPlayer.Name)
	end
	return PlayerList
end
MainLoop()

local SelectedPlayerName = nil
local PlayerSelectionDropdown = ChildTab:AddDropdown({
	["Name"] = "Selecione um player para perseguir",
	["Options"] = PlayerList,
	["Default"] = "",
	["Callback"] = function(PlayerName)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1690
		if game.Players:FindFirstChild(PlayerName) then
			SelectedPlayerName = PlayerName
		else
			SelectedPlayerName = nil
		end
	end
})
ChildTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Atualizar Player List",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1688, (ref) vu1692, (ref) vu1690
		local PlayerData = MainLoop()
		if PlayerSelectionDropdown and PlayerData then
			pcall(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1692, (ref) vu1693
				PlayerSelectionDropdown:Refresh(PlayerData)
			end)
			if SelectedPlayerName and not game.Players:FindFirstChild(SelectedPlayerName) then
				SelectedPlayerName = nil
				pcall(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) vu1692
					PlayerSelectionDropdown:Set("")
				end)
			end
		end
	end
})
game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1688, (ref) vu1692
	task.wait(0.1)
	local UpdatedData = MainLoop()
	if PlayerSelectionDropdown and UpdatedData then
		pcall(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1692, (ref) vu1694
			PlayerSelectionDropdown:Refresh(UpdatedData)
		end)
	end
end)
game.Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(LeavingPlayer)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1688, (ref) vu1692, (ref) vu1690
	task.wait(0.1)
	local CurrentData = MainLoop()
	if PlayerSelectionDropdown and CurrentData then
		pcall(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) vu1692, (ref) vu1696
			PlayerSelectionDropdown:Refresh(CurrentData)
		end)
		if SelectedPlayerName == LeavingPlayer.Name then
			SelectedPlayerName = nil
			pcall(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1692
				PlayerSelectionDropdown:Set("")
			end)
		end
	end
end)
ChildTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Enviar crian\195\167a",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1690, (ref) vu1682
		if SelectedPlayerName then
			if not (workspace:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name) and workspace[LocalPlayer.Name]:FindFirstChild("FollowCharacter")) then
				local FollowArguments = { "CharacterFollowSpawnPlayer", "BabyBoy" }
				local Success, ErrorMessage = pcall(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) vu1697
					game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Bab1yFollo1w"):FireServer(unpack(FollowArguments))
				end)
				if not Success then
					warn("Erro ao enviar crian\195\167a: " .. ErrorMessage)
				end
			end
			task.wait(0.2)
			if workspace:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name) then
				local Iterator, State, Index = pairs(workspace[LocalPlayer.Name]:GetChildren())
				while true do
					local ChildInstance
					Index, ChildInstance = Iterator(State, Index)
					if Index == nil then
						break
					end
					if ChildInstance:IsA("BasePart") then
						ChildInstance.CanCollide = true
					end
				end
			end
			local TargetCharacterName = SelectedPlayerName
			if workspace:FindFirstChild(TargetCharacterName) and (workspace:FindFirstChild(LocalPlayer.Name) and workspace[LocalPlayer.Name]:FindFirstChild("FollowCharacter")) then
				workspace[LocalPlayer.Name].FollowCharacter.Parent = workspace[TargetCharacterName]
				if rawget(getgenv(), "RunService") then
					return
				end
				getgenv().RunService = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) vu1704
					local FollowCharacter = workspace[TargetCharacterName]:FindFirstChild("FollowCharacter")
					local TargetTorso = FollowCharacter and FollowCharacter:FindFirstChild("Torso") and (FollowCharacter.Torso:FindFirstChild("BodyPosition") and workspace[TargetCharacterName]:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"))
					if TargetTorso then
						FollowCharacter.Torso.BodyPosition.Position = TargetTorso.Position - TargetTorso.CFrame.LookVector * 3
						FollowCharacter.Torso.BodyGyro.CFrame = TargetTorso.CFrame
					end
				end)
			end
		else
			warn("Nenhum jogador selecionado!")
		end
	end
})

	["Name"] = "Spectar Player",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(ToggleState)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1690
		local vu1714 = game:GetService("Players")
		local v1715 = game:GetService("RunService")
		local vu1716 = vu1714.LocalPlayer
		local vu1717 = workspace.CurrentCamera
		if ToggleState then
			if not SelectedPlayerName then
				warn("Nenhum jogador selecionado para spectar!")
				return false
			end
			if not rawget(getgenv(), "CameraConnection") then
				getgenv().CameraConnection = v1715.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) vu1714, (ref) vu1690, (ref) vu1717, (ref) vu1716
					local TargetPlayer = vu1714:FindFirstChild(SelectedPlayerName)
					if TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character and TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						vu1717.CameraSubject = TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid
					else
						if rawget(getgenv(), "CameraConnection") then
							getgenv().CameraConnection:Disconnect()
							getgenv().CameraConnection = nil
						end
						local CameraService = vu1717
						local HumanoidSubject
						if vu1716.Character then
							HumanoidSubject = vu1716.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") or nil
						else
							HumanoidSubject = nil
						end
						CameraService.CameraSubject = HumanoidSubject
					end
				end)
			end
		else
			if rawget(getgenv(), "CameraConnection") then
				getgenv().CameraConnection:Disconnect()
				getgenv().CameraConnection = nil
			end
			if vu1716.Character and vu1716.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
				vu1717.CameraSubject = vu1716.Character.Humanoid
			end
		end
	end
})

local ChatMessage = nil
local TextChatService = game:GetService("TextChatService")
local TargetTextChannel = TextChatService.ChatInputBarConfiguration
if TargetTextChannel then
	TargetTextChannel = TextChatService.ChatInputBarConfiguration.TargetTextChannel
end
function sendchat(ChatMessage)
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1729, (ref) vu1730
	if ChatMessage and ChatMessage ~= "" then
		if TextChatService.ChatVersion ~= Enum.ChatVersion.LegacyChatService then
			if TargetTextChannel then
				local SendSuccess, SendError = pcall(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) vu1730, (ref) pu1731
					TargetTextChannel:SendAsync(ChatMessage)
				end)
				if not SendSuccess then
					warn("Erro ao enviar chat: " .. SendError)
				end
			end
		else
			local LegacySendSuccess, LegacySendError = pcall(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) pu1731
				game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild("DefaultChatSystemChatEvents").SayMessageRequest:FireServer(ChatMessage, "All")
			end)
			if not LegacySendSuccess then
				warn("Erro ao enviar chat: " .. LegacySendError)
			end
		end
	end
end
PlayerTab:AddTextBox({

	["PlaceholderText"] = "Digite a mensagem",
	["Callback"] = function(MessageText)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1728
		ChatMessage = MessageText
	end
})
PlayerTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Send Chat",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1728

local SelectedPlayerName = nil
local SitConnection = nil
local PlayerDropdown = PlayerTab:AddDropdown({
	["Name"] = "Selecionar Player",
	["Default"] = "",
	["Options"] = PlayerList,
	["Callback"] = function(SelectedPlayerName)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1739

PlayerTab:AddToggle({
	["Name"] = "Head Sit (Cavalinho)",
	["Default"] = false,
	["Callback"] = function(IsToggled)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1739, (ref) vu1740
		local LocalPlayer = game.Players.LocalPlayer
		local LocalCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
		local HumanoidRootPart = LocalCharacter:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
		local Humanoid = LocalCharacter:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
		if not SelectedPlayerName or SelectedPlayerName == "" then
			warn("Nenhum jogador selecionado para Head Sit!")
			return false
		end
		local TargetPlayer = game.Players:FindFirstChild(SelectedPlayerName)
		if IsToggled then
			if not (TargetPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character) then
				warn("Jogador selecionado n\195\163o encontrado ou sem Character!")
				return false
			end
			Humanoid.Sit = true
			if SitConnection then
				SitConnection:Disconnect()
			end
			SitConnection = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function()
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1748, (ref) vu1747, (ref) vu1746, (ref) vu1740
				if TargetPlayer.Character and (TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") and Humanoid.Sit) then
					HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = TargetPlayer.Character.Head.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, 0) * CFrame.new(0, 1.6, 0.4)
				elseif SitConnection then
					SitConnection:Disconnect()
					SitConnection = nil
					Humanoid.Sit = false
				end
			end)
		else
			if SitConnection then
				SitConnection:Disconnect()
				SitConnection = nil
			end
			Humanoid.Sit = false
		end
	end
})
PlayerTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Atualizar tabela",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1688, (ref) vu1742, (ref) vu1739

			end)

				SelectedPlayerName = nil
				pcall(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) vu1742
					PlayerDropdown:Set("")
				end)
			end
		end
	end
})

ItemsTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Colorir Mapa Ch\195\163o [Muito OP]",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- block 166
		local ReplicatedTool = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Too1l")
		game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").ReplicatedEvents:FindFirstChild("1Clea1rTool1s")
		local OriginalRootCFrame = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
		local ToolOffsetVectors = {}
		local ToolName = "PaintRoller"
		local TotalTools = 100
		local IsAnchored = true
		for ToolIndex = 1, 100 do
			if ToolIndex == 1 then
				table.insert(ToolOffsetVectors, Vector3.new(0, 5, 0))
			else
				table.insert(ToolOffsetVectors, Vector3.new((ToolIndex - 1) * 1.2, 5, 0))
			end
		end
		local BackpackIterator, BackpackChildren, ToolIterator = pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren())
		local ToolCount = 0
		while true do
			local CurrentTool
			ToolIterator, CurrentTool = BackpackIterator(BackpackChildren, ToolIterator)
			if ToolIterator == nil then
				break
			end
			if CurrentTool:IsA("Tool") and CurrentTool.Name == ToolName then
				ToolCount = ToolCount + 1
			end
		end
		local CharacterIterator, CharacterChildren, Child = pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetChildren())
		while true do
			local ChildInstance
			Child, ChildInstance = CharacterIterator(CharacterChildren, Child)
			if Child == nil then
				break
			end
			if ChildInstance:IsA("Tool") and ChildInstance.Name == ToolName then
				ToolCount = ToolCount + 1
			end
		end
		if TotalTools <= ToolCount then
			local ChildIterator, ChildTable, ChildKey = pairs(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetChildren())
			while true do
				local Tool
				ChildKey, Tool = ChildIterator(ChildTable, ChildKey)
				if ChildKey == nil then

			end
		end
		EquiparTudo()
		wait(1)
		EquiparTudo()
		wait(1)
		EquiparTudo()
		function startSpin()
			local PlayersService = game:GetService("Players")
			local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
			local LocalPlayer = PlayersService.LocalPlayer
			local HumanoidRootPart = (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()):WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
			task.wait(1)
			local RotationRadians = math.rad(1750)
			RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(DeltaTime)
				-- upvalues: (ref) vu1919, (ref) vu1920
				HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(0, RotationRadians * DeltaTime, 0)
			end)
		end
		startSpin()
		-- ::l42::
		return
	end
})
local SelectedColor = ToolColors[1].Color
local function UpdateCharacterColors()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1922
	local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
	local Backpack = LocalPlayer.Backpack
	local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
	local ColorArguments = { SelectedColor }
	local function ProcessChild(ChildInstance)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1926
		local IsPaintRollerTool = ChildInstance:IsA("Tool") and (ChildInstance.Name == "PaintRoller" and ChildInstance:FindFirstChild("SetColor", true))
		if IsPaintRollerTool then
			IsPaintRollerTool:FireServer(unpack(ColorArguments))
		end
	end
	local ChildIterator, ChildIndex, ChildValue = ipairs(Backpack:GetChildren())
	while true do
		local CurrentValue
		ChildValue, CurrentValue = ChildIterator(ChildIndex, ChildValue)
		if ChildValue == nil then
			break
		end
		ProcessChild(CurrentValue)
	end
	local ChildIterator, ChildList, Index = ipairs(Character:GetChildren())
	while true do
		local ChildInstance
		Index, ChildInstance = ChildIterator(ChildList, Index)
		if Index == nil then
			break
		end
		ProcessChild(ChildInstance)
	end
end
local function CallbackFunction(Callback)
	local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
	local Backpack = LocalPlayer.Backpack
	local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
	local function TransferTools()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1941, (ref) vu1942
		local BackpackChildren = Backpack
		local IteratorFunction, CurrentChild, ChildIndex = ipairs(BackpackChildren:GetChildren())
		while true do
			local ChildInstance
			ChildIndex, ChildInstance = IteratorFunction(CurrentChild, ChildIndex)
			if ChildIndex == nil then
				break
			end
			if ChildInstance:IsA("Tool") and ChildInstance.Name == "PaintRoller" then
				ChildInstance.Parent = Character
			end
		end
	end;
	(function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1942, (ref) vu1941
		local PlayerBackpack = Character
		local BackpackIterator, BackpackChild, Index = ipairs(PlayerBackpack:GetChildren())
		while true do
			local ChildOrTool
			Index, ChildOrTool = BackpackIterator(BackpackChild, Index)
			if Index == nil then
				break
			end
			if ChildOrTool:IsA("Tool") and ChildOrTool.Name == "PaintRoller" then
				ChildOrTool.Parent = Backpack
			end
		end
	end)()
	wait(0.7)
	if Callback then
		Callback()
	end
	wait(0.7)
	TransferTools()
end

local function ApplyColorsToTools()
	-- upvalues: (ref) vu1757
	local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
	local Backpack = LocalPlayer.Backpack
	local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
	local ColorCount = #ToolColors
	local BackpackIterator, Child, Index = ipairs(Backpack:GetChildren())
	local PaintRollerCount = 0
	local function ApplyPaintToTool(ToolInstance, ColorToApply)
		local SetColorRemoteEvent = ToolInstance:IsA("Tool") and (ToolInstance.Name == "PaintRoller" and ToolInstance:FindFirstChild("SetColor", true))
		if SetColorRemoteEvent then
			SetColorRemoteEvent:FireServer(ColorToApply)
		end
	end
	while true do
		local ChildTool
		Index, ChildTool = BackpackIterator(Child, Index)
		if Index == nil then
			break
		end
		if ChildTool.Name == "PaintRoller" then
			PaintRollerCount = PaintRollerCount + 1
			ApplyPaintToTool(ChildTool, ToolColors[(PaintRollerCount - 1) % ColorCount + 1].Color)
		end
	end
	local ChildIterator, Child, Index = ipairs(Character:GetChildren())
	while true do
		local ChildInstance
		Index, ChildInstance = ChildIterator(Child, Index)
		if Index == nil then
			break
		end
		if ChildInstance.Name == "PaintRoller" then
			PaintRollerCount = PaintRollerCount + 1
			ApplyPaintToTool(ChildInstance, ToolColors[(PaintRollerCount - 1) % ColorCount + 1].Color)
		end
	end
end
ItemsTab:AddButton({
	["Name"] = "Colorido",
	["Callback"] = function()
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1954, (ref) vu1982
		CallbackFunction(ApplyColorsToTools)
	end
})

local CombinedItems = {}
while true do
	local CurrentItem
	IteratorIndex, CurrentItem = Iterator(Element, IteratorIndex)
	if IteratorIndex == nil then
		break
	end
	local IteratorFunction, IteratorState, IteratorIndex = ipairs(PlayerList)
	local CurrentIndex = IteratorIndex
	while true do
		local SecondColor
		IteratorIndex, SecondColor = IteratorFunction(IteratorState, IteratorIndex)
		if IteratorIndex == nil then
			break
		end
		if CurrentIndex ~= IteratorIndex then
			table.insert(CombinedItems, {
				["Name"] = CurrentItem.Name .. " e " .. SecondColor.Name,
				["Colors"] = { CurrentItem.Color, SecondColor.Color }
			})
		end
	end
end

			if CurrentPairIndex == nil then
				break
			end
			table.insert(CombinedColorNames, PlayerName.Name)
		end
		return CombinedColorNames
	end)(),
	["Default"] = CombinedItems[1].Name,
	["Callback"] = function(SelectedOption)
		-- upvalues: (ref) vu1988, (ref) vu1986

				break

					-- upvalues: (ref) vu2004
					local LocalPlayer = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
					local Backpack = LocalPlayer.Backpack
					local Character = LocalPlayer.Character
					local Colors = Option.Colors
					local Iterator, Table, ChildIndex = ipairs(Backpack:GetChildren())
					local PaintRollerCount = 0
					local function ColorizePaintRoller(ToolInstance, ColorValue)
						local SetColorEvent = ToolInstance:IsA("Tool") and (ToolInstance.Name == "PaintRoller" and ToolInstance:FindFirstChild("SetColor", true))
						if SetColorEvent then
							SetColorEvent:FireServer(ColorValue)
						end
					end
					while true do
						local FoundTool
						ChildIndex, FoundTool = Iterator(Table, ChildIndex)
						if ChildIndex == nil then
							break
						end
						if FoundTool.Name == "PaintRoller" then
							PaintRollerCount = PaintRollerCount + 1
							ColorizePaintRoller(FoundTool, Colors[(PaintRollerCount - 1) % 2 + 1])
						end
					end
					local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, ChildIndex = ipairs(Character:GetChildren())
					while true do
						local CurrentChild
						ChildIndex, CurrentChild = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, ChildIndex)
						if ChildIndex == nil then
							break
						end
						if CurrentChild.Name == "PaintRoller" then
							PaintRollerCount = PaintRollerCount + 1
							ColorizePaintRoller(CurrentChild, Colors[(PaintRollerCount - 1) % 2 + 1])
						end
					end
				end)
				break
			end
		end
	end

			local CurrentTool
			ToolIndex, CurrentTool = NextToolPair(ToolIteratorState, ToolIndex)
			if ToolIndex == nil then
				break
			end
			if CurrentTool:IsA("Tool") then
				CurrentTool.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				local SelectedToolName = ToolPositions[math.min(ToolIndex, #ToolPositions)]
				if CurrentTool:IsDescendantOf(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character) then
					CurrentTool.GripPos = SelectedToolName
				else
					warn("", CurrentTool.Name, "")
				end
			end
		end
		return
	end
